TL;DR: 本文提出SplAttN，通过将传统的硬投影替换为可微高斯点阵（Differentiable Gaussian Splatting），解决了点云补全中多模态连接因稀疏支持导致的跨模态熵崩溃问题。该方法生成稠密连续的图像平面表示，增强梯度传播与跨模态学习能力，在PCN、ShapeNet-55/34上达到当前最优性能，并在KITTI真实场景数据集上验证了其对视觉线索的稳健依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在点云补全中依赖多模态信息，但标准硬投影导致图像平面表示过于稀疏，破坏了跨模态连接，引发跨模态熵崩溃，限制了视觉先验的传播和模型性能。

Method: 提出SplAttN，用可微高斯点阵替代硬投影，将投影过程建模为连续密度估计，生成稠密且连续的图像平面表征，从而维持跨模态连接与梯度流动。

Result: 在PCN、ShapeNet-55/34数据集上达到状态领先性能；在KITTI真实世界基准测试中，相较于基线方法退化为仅依赖模板的单模态模型，SplAttN仍保持对视觉信息的强依赖，验证了其有效的跨模态连接能力。

Conclusion: 通过可微高斯点阵实现稠密连续的投影表示，SplAttN有效缓解了跨模态熵崩溃问题，显著提升了多模态点云补全中跨模态信息的利用效率与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Although multi-modal learning has advanced point cloud completion, the theoretical mechanisms remain unclear. Recent works attribute success to the connection between modalities, yet we identify that standard hard projection severs this connection: projecting a sparse point cloud onto the image plane yields an extremely sparse support, which hinders visual prior propagation, a failure mode we term Cross-Modal Entropy Collapse. To address this practical limitation, we propose SplAttN, which replaces hard projection with Differentiable Gaussian Splatting to produce a dense, continuous image-plane representation. By reformulating projection as continuous density estimation, SplAttN avoids collapsed sparse support, facilitates gradient flow, and improves cross-modal connection learnability. Extensive experiments show that SplAttN achieves state-of-the-art performance on PCN and ShapeNet-55/34. Crucially, we utilize the real-world KITTI benchmark as a stress test for multi-modal reliance. Counter-factual evaluation reveals that while baselines degenerate into unimodal template retrievers insensitive to visual removal, SplAttN maintains a robust dependency on visual cues, validating that our method establishes an effective cross-modal connection. Code is available at https://github.com/zay002/SplAttN.

</details>


### [48] [Decision Boundary-aware Generation for Long-tailed Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01468)
*Jiacheng Yang,Ruichi Zhang,Chikai Shang,Mengke Li,Xinyi Shang,Junlong Gao,Yonggang Zhang,Yang Lu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出决策边界感知生成（DBG）框架，旨在解决长尾数据分布中尾类准确率低的问题。现有方法如基于扩散的生成增强和头到尾迁移虽能缓解分类器偏差，但引入了非局部特征混杂，导致类别间决策边界重叠和分布偏移。DBG通过生成靠近决策边界的有信息样本，促进近边界表征学习，从而在不增加类别间混淆的前提下实现更清晰的决策空间，显著提升尾类与整体准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长尾数据导致分类器偏向头部类别，降低尾部类别准确率；现有生成增强与迁移方法虽缓解偏差，但引发特征混杂与边界模糊问题，需更精细的生成策略以维持类别可分性。

Method: 提出决策边界感知生成（DBG）框架，通过识别边界模糊问题，生成具有判别性的近边界样本，强化模型对边界区域的表征能力，从而优化决策空间结构。

Result: 在多个标准长尾基准上，DBG consistently 提升尾类与整体准确率，减少类别间重叠，有效改善长尾学习性能。

Conclusion: DBG 通过生成近边界样本，实现了长尾数据的再平衡与更清晰的决策边界，为长尾学习提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Long-tailed data bias decision boundaries toward head classes and degrade tail class accuracy. Diffusion-based generative augmentation address this problem by generating additional data, while head-to-tail transfer further mitigate the generator bias inherit from long-tailed dataset. However, we show that while head-to-tail transfer helps balance the decision space of the classifier, it also induces latent non-local feature mixing that entangles inter-class features, causing decision boundary overlap and tail class distribution shift. To address this, we first identify the problem of boundary ambiguity and then propose Decision Boundary-aware Generation (DBG) framework, which promotes near-boundary representation learning by generating informative near-boundary samples. Overall, DBG rebalances the long-tailed dataset while yielding more separable decision space for long-tailed learning. Across standard long-tailed benchmarks, DBG consistently improves tail class and overall accuracy with less inter-class overlap. The code of DBG is available at https://github.com/keepdigitalabc-svg/DBG.

### [49] [LIE: LiDAR-only HD Map Construction with Intensity Enhancement via Online Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01478)
*Kanak Mazumder,Fabian B. Flohr*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 摄像头缺乏深度信息，难以准确还原场景几何；而LiDAR虽有精确3D测量但缺少密集语义和纹理信息，因此需要一种无需依赖摄像头、能充分利用LiDAR数据进行语义地图构建的方法。

Method: 采用知识蒸馏（KD）机制，设计教师分支融合学生端的LiDAR特征与对应的2D强度图块，以提供密集监督信号，实现在线蒸馏，从而增强LiDAR-only语义分割性能。

Result: 在nuScenes数据集上，LIE方法相比单模态方法显著提升性能，较最先进摄像头模型提高8.2% mIoU；在长距离、复杂环境条件下表现稳定；在Argoverse2上仅用10%数据微调即超越全量训练的摄像头模型。

Conclusion: LIE是一种高效的纯LiDAR语义地图构建方法，克服了单一传感器的局限性，实现了高性能、强鲁棒性和良好泛化能力，为自动驾驶中的高精地图生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Online High-Definition (HD) map construction is a key component of autonomous driving. Recent methods rely on multi-view camera images for cost-effective HD map segmentation, but cameras lack depth information for accurate scene geometry. In contrast, LiDAR provides precise 3D measurements but lacks dense semantic cues. In this work, we propose LIE, LiDAR-only semantic map construction method that employ Knowledge Distillation (KD) to handle the lack of dense semantic and texture cues. Specifically, the teacher branch fuses student LiDAR features and the corresponding 2D intensity map tile to provide dense supervision for segmenting map elements using online distillation scheme. Experimental results show that our method outperforms all single-modality approaches, achieving 8.2% higher mIoU than the state-of-the-art camera-based model on nuScenes. LIE is robust over long ranges and under challenging weather and lighting, and efficiently adapts to Argoverse2 with only 10% fine-tuning, surpassing camera-based models trained on the full dataset. Source code will be available \href{https://iv.ee.hm.edu/lie/}{here}.

### [50] [CSGuard: Toward Forgery-Resistant Watermarking in Diffusion Models via Compressed Sensing Constraint](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01479)
*Jiewei Lai,Lan Zhang,Chen Tang,Pengcheng Sun,Zhaopeng Zhang,Yunhao Wang,Hui Jin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CSGuard 是首个抵抗伪造攻击的基于压缩感知的隐式扩散模型水印方案，通过秘密矩阵绑定图像生成与验证过程，确保仅持有密钥的用户可正确嵌入或验证水印，有效防止非法用户伪造，同时保持生成质量和水印完整性。实验表明其将攻击成功率从100.0%降至28.12%，对正常水印图像检测率达100%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于潜在空间的扩散模型水印方法易受伪造攻击，攻击者可通过反向重构水印图像并使用任意提示词重新生成，实现恶意内容的虚假归属，亟需一种能抵抗此类攻击的鲁棒水印机制。

Method: 提出 CSGuard 水印方案，利用压缩感知技术将水印嵌入与图像生成/验证过程绑定至一个秘密矩阵，只有拥有该矩阵的合法用户才能正确嵌入或验证水印，从而阻止未经授权的伪造行为。

Result: 实验结果显示，CSGuard 将伪造攻击的成功率从 100.0% 显著降低至 28.12%，对合法水印图像的检测率达到 100%，且未牺牲生成质量或水印有效性。

Conclusion: CSGuard 成功实现了对伪造攻击的强防御能力，为扩散模型生成内容提供了安全可靠的内容溯源机制，兼具高安全性、高可用性与良好的兼容性。

Abstract: Latent-based diffusion model watermarking embeds watermarks into generated images' latent space to enable content attribution, offering a training-free solution for intellectual property protection and digital forensics. However, these methods exhibit a critical vulnerability to the forgery attack, attackers can extract the watermark by inverting the watermarked image and re-generating it with an arbitrary prompt, thereby enabling false attribution on malicious content. In this paper, we propose the CSGuard, the first forgery-resistant watermarking schema that leverages compressed sensing to bind the watermarked image generation and verification to a secret matrix. This ensures that only users possessing the secret matrix can correctly embed or verify the image watermark, prevents the illegal users from forgery without compromising generation quality and watermark integrity. Experimental results demonstrate that CSGuard achieves strong forgery resistance, reduces the attack success rate from 100.0\% to 28.12\%, and achieve 100\% detection rate on benign watermarked images without compromising watermarking effectiveness.

### [51] [AttnRouter: Per-Category Attention Routing for Training-Free Image Editing on MMDiT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01480)
*Guandong Li,Mengxia Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究了在Qwen-Image-Edit-2511（一个60层的多模态扩散Transformer）上无需训练的图像编辑方法，提出三种贡献：(i) 提出KVInject，一种单次前向注意力操作，通过局部层/步带将源图像一半的键值投影混合到噪声一半中，比传统两步MasaCtrl更简单且避免提示不匹配问题；(ii) 发现不同编辑类型无单一主导注意力操作，提出AttnRouter，基于类别路由选择最优操作，使用真实标签时提升复合评分6.4%，即使使用零样本分类器也接近该性能；(iii) 通过层、步、alpha的消融实验定位有效编辑子电路：早期去噪步骤（S0-7）和早期层（L0-15）的注入最有效，而晚期层无效，α在[0.3, 0.5]区间表现最佳。同时揭示了从UNet经验中不适用的结论，如简单的K/V缩放无法超越基线，激进变体导致生成崩溃。代码、路由表及数据集已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练-free图像编辑方法在多模态扩散模型（如MMDiT）上存在效率低、提示不匹配等问题，尤其在复杂架构下难以稳定生效。本文旨在探索高效、鲁棒且可解释的编辑机制，突破传统方法局限。

Method: 提出KVInject实现单次前向注意力修改，通过控制键值投影的混合比例实现编辑；设计AttnRouter根据编辑类型动态选择最优操作；结合层、步、参数α的系统性消融分析，定位关键编辑子电路。

Result: KVInject显著优于MasaCtrl，在复合评分上避免31%下降；AttnRouter在真实标签下提升6.4%，零样本分类器闭合98%差距；早期步骤（S0-7）与早期层（L0-15）注入效果最佳，α∈[0.3,0.5]为稳定最优区间；简单缩放无效，激进调整导致生成崩溃。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了多模态扩散模型中有效编辑的关键机制：局部、早期、适度的注意力注入是成功的核心。所提方法在无需训练前提下实现了高效、鲁棒的图像编辑，并为未来研究提供了可解释的实践路径。

Abstract: We study training-free image editing on Qwen-Image-Edit-2511, a 60-block multi-modal diffusion transformer (MMDiT) that concatenates noise and source-image tokens within a single attention stream. We make three contributions. (i) We introduce KVInject, a single-forward attention manipulation that alpha-blends source-half key/value projections into the noise-half within a localized layer/step band. KVInject is simpler than the classical two-pass MasaCtrl recipe and avoids the prompt-mismatch failure mode that disables MasaCtrl on MMDiT (composite score drops 31% versus baseline). (ii) We show that no single attention operation dominates across edit types, motivating AttnRouter, a per-category routing table that dispatches edits to the operation that best preserves source structure for that type. With ground-truth categories the router improves the CLIP-T+DINO-I composite by 6.4% over the editing baseline; an automatic CLIP zero-shot classifier closes 98% of this gap despite only 55% category accuracy. (iii) Through layer-, step-, and alpha-band ablations we localize the editing-effective attention sub-circuit: K/V injection in early denoising steps (S0-7) recovers nearly all of the gain of full-step injection, while injection in early (L0-15) or late (L45-60) layer bands fails to drive editing entirely; alpha in [0.3, 0.5] is a stable sweet spot. We also report negative results that highlight what does not transfer from the UNet folklore: simple K/V rescaling never beats baseline and aggressive variants collapse generation entirely (composite 0.084). We release code, pre-computed routing tables, and a 100-sample stratified subset of ImgEdit-Bench used in all ablations.

### [52] [CGFformer: Cluster-Guidance Frequency Transformer for Pansharpening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01490)
*Zijian Zhou,Jianing Zhang,Kai Sun,Xiangyu Zhao,Chunxia Zhang,Xiangyong Cao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CGFformer，一种基于聚类引导的频率Transformer模型，用于解决当前基于频率的图像融合方法中固定滤波器无法适应复杂频率分布的问题。通过自适应分离模块结合K-means聚类实现高低频成分精准分离，引入双流精炼模块与Transformer交叉注意力机制有效抑制多种噪声，设计频率-空间融合模块增强细节并促进空间-频率交互，显著提升融合图像质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有主流基于频率的超分辨率融合方法使用固定频率滤波器，难以适应潘宁图像和多光谱图像中复杂的、空间多样化的频率分布；同时现有去噪策略未能充分挖掘频率成分，对不同类型噪声的抑制效果不佳。

Method: 设计自适应分离模块，利用K-means聚类融合局部特征与非局部信息以精确分离高频与低频成分；引入双流精炼模块结合Transformer交叉注意力机制，联合抑制相关与无关频率干扰；构建频率-空间融合模块，增强细节并促进空间与频率间的交互，实现更优的空间结构重建。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上的大量实验表明，所提出的CGFformer在图像融合性能上显著优于现有方法，有效提升了高分辨率多光谱图像的生成质量。

Conclusion: CGFformer通过聚类引导的自适应频率处理与跨模态交互机制，成功解决了频率分布不均及噪声抑制不足的问题，为遥感图像融合提供了高效且鲁棒的新框架。

Abstract: Pansharpening aims to generate high-resolution multispectral (HRMS) images by fusing low-resolution multispectral (LRMS) images with high-resolution panchromatic (PAN) images. However, the current mainstream frequency-based pansharpening methods employ fixed frequency filters, which cannot precisely adapt to complex and spatially diversified frequency distributions in PAN and MS images. Furthermore, existing denoising strategies insufficiently exploit frequency components for denoising and struggle to suppress various noise types accurately. To address these challenges, we propose CGFformer, a cluster-guidance frequency Transformer that focuses on varying frequency distribution and interactions between frequency and spatial components. Specifically, we design an adaptive separation module that integrates local features and non-local information through K-means clustering, enabling more precise separation of high- and low-frequency components. Subsequently, we introduce a dual-stream refinement module combined with Transformer-based cross-attention to remove various noise, allowing the network to jointly suppress frequency-relevant and irrelevant disturbances. In addition, we develop a frequency-spatial fusion module designed to enhance detail and facilitate spatial-frequency interaction, ensuring more effective reconstruction of spatial structures in the fused results. Extensive experiments on multiple benchmark datasets demonstrate that the proposed CGFformer achieves notable improvements over existing pansharpening approaches.

### [53] [SF20K Competition 2025: Summary and findings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01496)
*Ridouane Ghermi,Xi Wang,Vicky Kalogeiton,Ivan Laptev*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该报告介绍了在ICCV 2025 SLoMO研讨会期间举办的首届短片20K（SF20K）竞赛的成果，旨在推动故事级视频理解超越短片段动作识别，引入基于业余短片语料库的开放式视频问答任务。通过使用基于GPT-4.1-nano的LLM-QA-Eval进行评估，竞赛吸引了22支队伍和286次提交，分为主赛道（无模型大小限制）和特设赛道（模型小于80亿参数）。主赛道冠军达65.7%准确率，特设赛道为48.7%，而人类表现上限为91.7%。分析显示：注重叙事的逐镜头处理优于均匀采帧；设计良好的多阶段小模型流水线可媲美甚至超过30倍以上的大模型端到端推理；字幕质量是影响性能的关键因素。结果表明，长视频问答的主要瓶颈在于信息选择与推理结构而非模型容量，当前方法与人类叙事理解仍有显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推动故事级视频理解从短片段动作识别向更复杂的长视频叙事理解演进，避免模型依赖对流行电影的记忆，强调多模态理解能力。

Method: 构建基于业余短片的开放式视频问答任务，采用SF20K-Test基准（95部影片，979个问答对），使用基于GPT-4.1-nano的自动化评估工具LLM-QA-Eval进行评分，设置主赛道与特设赛道以对比不同规模模型的表现。

Result: 主赛道最高准确率为65.7%，特设赛道为48.7%，人类表现上限为91.7%；研究表明，叙事感知的逐镜头处理优于均匀采样；小模型多阶段流水线可媲美甚至超越大模型端到端推理；字幕质量显著影响性能。

Conclusion: 当前长视频问答的核心挑战并非模型容量，而是信息选择与推理结构的设计；尽管取得进展，但现有方法与人类水平的叙事理解之间仍存在显著差距。

Abstract: This report presents the results and findings of the first edition of the Short-Films 20K (SF20K) Competition, held in conjunction with the SLoMO Workshop at ICCV 2025. The competition is designed to advance story-level video understanding beyond short-clip action recognition, introducing an open-ended video question-answering task built on a corpus of amateur short films. This setup ensures that models must rely on multimodal understanding rather than memorization of popular movies. Evaluation is conducted using the SF20K-Test benchmark (95 movies, 979 question-answer pairs) and scored via LLM-QA-Eval, an automated judge based on GPT-4.1-nano. The competition attracted 22 teams and 286 submissions across two tracks: a Main Track with unrestricted model size and a Special Track limited to models under 8 billion parameters. The winning team achieved 65.7% accuracy on the Main Track and 48.7% on the Special Track, against a human performance ceiling of 91.7%. Our analysis reveals several key findings: narrative-aware, shot-level processing consistently outperforms uniform frame sampling; well-designed multi-stage pipelines using smaller models can match or exceed end-to-end inference with models over 30x larger; and subtitle quality is a dominant factor in performance. These results highlight that the primary bottleneck in long-form video QA lies in information selection and reasoning structure rather than raw model capacity, and that a substantial gap remains between current methods and human-level narrative comprehension.

### [54] [Towards Visual Query Localization in the 3D World](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01498)
*Liang Peng,Bohan Tan,Zhipeng Zhang,Haobo Li,Yifan Jiao,Xingping Dong,Libo Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文首次提出3D视觉查询定位任务，并引入首个3D多模态基准数据集3DVQL，包含2,002个序列、约17万帧和6.4K个响应轨迹段，涵盖38类物体。数据集提供点云、RGB图像和深度图像等多种模态，且经过多轮人工标注与验证以确保高质量。实验表明现有方法在不同融合模块上表现差异显著，为此提出新型融合算法LaF，性能显著优于基线模型。相关代码与数据将公开发布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉查询定位研究主要集中在2D视频，而3D空间中的该任务尚未受到足够关注，亟需一个专门的基准数据集来推动该方向的发展。

Method: 提出3DVQL基准数据集，包含多模态数据（点云、RGB、深度图），并设计基于点云与RGB图像的多模态融合基线模型；进一步提出一种名为LaF的提升-注意力融合算法，用于有效整合多模态特征。

Result: 实验结果显示，现有方法在不同融合策略下表现差异明显；所提出的LaF算法在多个指标上显著超越基线模型，展现出更强的性能。

Conclusion: 3DVQL是首个面向3D多模态视觉查询定位的基准数据集，具有高精度标注和丰富模态支持，能够有效推动该领域的研究发展。所提出的LaF模型为未来方法设计提供了新思路，相关资源已开源。

Abstract: Visual query localization (VQL) aims to predict the spatio-temporal response of the most recent occurrence in a sequence given a query. Currently, most research focuses on visual query localization in 2D videos, while its counterpart in 3D space has received little attention. In this paper, we make the first attempt to address visual query localization in the 3D world by introducing a novel benchmark, dubbed 3DVQL. Specifically, 3DVQL contains 2,002 sequences with around 170,000 frames and 6.4K response track segments from 38 object categories. Each sequence in 3DVQL is provided with multiple modalities, including point clouds, RGB images, and depth images, to support flexible research. To ensure high-quality annotations, each sequence is manually annotated with multiple rounds of verification and refinement. To the best of our knowledge, 3DVQL is the first benchmark for 3D multimodal visual query localization. To facilitate comparison in subsequent research, we implement a series of representative 3D multimodal VQL baselines using point clouds and RGB images. The experimental results show that existing methods exhibit significant performance variations across different fusion modules. To encourage future research, we propose a lift-and-attention fusion algorithm named LaF, which significantly outperforms existing baseline models. Our benchmark and model will be publicly released at https://github.com/wuhengliangliang/3DVQL.

</details>


### [55] [SwiftPie: Lightning-fast Subject-driven Image Personalization via One step Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01510)
*Huy Duong,Trong-Tung Nguyen,Cuong Pham,Anh Tran,Khoi Nguyen,Minh Hoai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SwiftPie 是首个一步扩散图像个性化工具，通过双分支身份注入机制和掩码引导的缩放策略，在单步扩散过程中实现快速、高质量的个性化图像生成，显著提升实时应用中的生成速度与性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像个性化方法依赖计算密集型微调、迭代优化或多步去噪过程，限制了其在实时应用中的部署与交互能力。

Method: 提出双分支身份注入机制和掩码引导的缩放策略，将主体身份信息高效融入单步扩散模型中。

Result: SwiftPie 在保持与多步方法相当的身份保真度和提示对齐能力的同时，实现了极快的生成速度，适用于实时个性化图像生成。

Conclusion: SwiftPie 为实时、高质量的个性化图像生成开辟了新路径，推动了交互式视觉合成的发展。

Abstract: Diffusion models have achieved remarkable success in high-quality image synthesis, sparking interest in image-guided generation tasks such as subject-driven image personalization. Despite their impressive personalization results, existing methods typically rely on computationally intensive fine-tuning, iterative optimization, or multi-step denoising processes, which significantly hinder their deployment and interactive capability in real-time applications. In this work, we present SwiftPie, the first one-step diffusion image personalization tool that enables lightning-fast generation of personalized images. SwiftPie introduces a novel dual-branch identity injection mechanism that effectively integrates subject identity into a one-step diffusion model. In addition, we incorporate a mask-guided rescaling strategy to further enhance subject contextualization within a single diffusion step. Extensive experiments demonstrate that SwiftPie not only delivers superior image personalization speed but also achieves comparable performance with multi-step approaches in both identity fidelity and prompt alignment. This work opens new opportunities for real-time, high-quality personalized image generation, paving the way for interactive visual synthesis.

### [56] [Two-Pass Zero-Shot Temporal-Spatial Grounding of Rare Traffic Events in Surveillance Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01512)
*Jiantang Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种无需微调的流水线，利用冻结的视觉-语言模型实现交通事故在时间、空间和碰撞类型上的联合定位。通过粗到精的两阶段分解和专家角色分配策略，在真实CCTV视频数据集ACCIDENT@CVPR 2026上取得0.539的ACC^S得分，显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交通事故在真实CCTV视频中的标注数据稀缺，但需精确联合定位事故的时间、空间位置及碰撞类型，传统微调方法受限于数据隐私与标注成本，因此需要一种无需微调且高效准确的解决方案。

Method: 采用粗到精的两阶段处理：第一阶段以1 fps全视频扫描生成粗略的（时间、空间、类型）估计；第二阶段在±3秒窗口内以5 fps细化，结合确定性置信度门控机制确保边界稳定性；同时引入角色分工，由Qwen3-VL-Plus负责定位，Gemini 3.1 Flash-Lite负责类型识别。

Result: 在ACCIDENT@CVPR 2026基准上达到ACC^S = 0.539（95% CI [0.525, 0.553]），相比基准论文最优基线提升0.127，相比最强单个视觉-语言模型基线提升0.143，相比朴素基线提升0.250；整体流程每视频最多调用三次API，约17%视频依赖物理推理兜底，总成本约$20。

Conclusion: 所提出的无微调流水线有效解决了真实场景下交通事故联合定位难题，兼具高精度与低成本，为实际部署提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Grounding traffic accidents in real CCTV footage is a rare-event problem where training on labeled accident video is often prohibited, yet accurate joint localization in time, space, and collision type is required. We present a no-fine-tuning pipeline that elicits this joint output from frozen vision-language models through two ideas. First, a coarse-to-fine two-pass decomposition: a full-video pass at 1 fps produces a coarse (t, x, y, c) tuple, then a second pass at 5 fps within a +/- 3 s window refines time and location, with two deterministic confidence gates that revert to the coarse estimate on boundary hedges or edge-clamped coordinates. Second, a specialist role assignment: Qwen3-VL-Plus handles grounding, Gemini 3.1 Flash-Lite handles typing on a centered video clip. On the ACCIDENT@CVPR 2026 benchmark (2,027 real CCTV videos) we reach ACC^S = 0.539 (95% CI [0.525, 0.553]): +0.127 over the benchmark paper's best-of-baselines oracle (0.412), +0.143 over the strongest single-VLM baseline (Molmo-7B, 0.396), and +0.250 over the naive baseline (0.289). The VLM path uses up to three API calls per video (17% fall back to physics on API failures); the full run costs ~$20.

</details>


### [57] [MIRL: Mutual Information-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01520)
*Yin Zhang,Jiaxuan Zhao,Zonghan Wu,Zengxiang Li,Junfeng Fang,Kun Wang,Qingsong Wen,Yilei Shao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MIRL 是一种解耦框架，通过利用生成描述与视觉输入之间的互信息（MI）作为低成本预筛选信号，解决现有强化学习中可验证奖励（RLVR）方法在轨迹采样浪费和奖励稀疏性方面的局限。该方法通过分叉策略智能分配采样预算，并独立优化视觉感知阶段，显著提升复杂视觉语言推理任务的准确率。在六个基准测试中，MIRL 达到 70.22% 的平均准确率，仅用 10 个预采样样本（选择前 6 个）即超越使用 16 个完整轨迹的性能，节省 25% 的计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 RLVR 方法在复杂视觉语言推理任务中受限于：大量采样预算浪费在因早期视觉描述错误而注定失败的轨迹上；稀疏奖励无法区分失败是由视觉感知还是推理阶段导致。因此需要一种更高效、可解耦的优化机制。

Method: 提出 MIRL 框架，利用生成描述与视觉输入间的互信息（MI）作为预筛选信号，实现对高潜力轨迹的智能筛选与预算分配（通过分叉策略）。同时采用解耦训练机制，为视觉感知阶段提供独立的 MI 奖励信号，克服奖励盲区问题。

Result: 在六个视觉语言推理基准测试中，MIRL 实现 70.22% 的平均准确率；仅使用 10 个预采样样本（选前 6 个）即可超越使用 16 个完整轨迹的性能，减少 25% 的完整轨迹采样需求。

Conclusion: MIRL 通过引入互信息驱动的预筛选与解耦训练，有效缓解了视觉感知错误和奖励稀疏性问题，在保持高性能的同时显著降低采样成本，为视觉语言模型的可靠推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) frequently suffer from visual perception errors and hallucinations that compromise answer accuracy in complex reasoning tasks. Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) offers a promising solution by optimizing policies using answer correctness signals. Despite their effectiveness, prevailing RLVR methods face two critical limitations. First, much of the sampling budget is wasted on trajectories doomed to fail due to early visual description errors. Second, sparse rewards cannot distinguish whether failures stem from visual perception or reasoning stages. We introduce MIRL, a decoupled framework that addresses both limitations by leveraging mutual information (MI) between generated descriptions and visual inputs as a cheap pre-screening signal. This enables intelligent budget allocation toward high-potential trajectories via forking, while decoupled training provides independent MI-based rewards for visual perception optimization, resolving reward blindness. Experiments on six vision-language reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that MIRL achieves 70.22% average accuracy and successfully surpasses the performance of sampling 16 complete trajectories using only 10 pre-samples with top-6 selection (25% fewer complete trajectories). Our code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/mirl-main/.

</details>

### [58] [H-Probes: Extracting Hierarchical Structures From Latent Representations of Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00847)
*Cutter Dawes,Aryan Sharma,Angelos Ioannis Lagos,Shivam Raval*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出H-probes，一种用于从大语言模型的隐状态中提取层次结构（如深度和成对距离）的线性探测工具。在合成树遍历任务中，H-probes能有效识别出包含层次结构信息的低维子空间，且这些子空间对任务性能具有因果重要性，并具备域内与跨域泛化能力。此外，在数学推理轨迹等真实层次任务中也发现了类似但较弱的层次结构。结果表明，模型不仅在语法和概念层面表示层次结构，还在更深层的抽象层面——包括推理过程本身——进行层次表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究虽表明大语言模型在多种需要层次推理的任务中表现良好，但对其如何在隐空间中几何化地表示层次结构缺乏深入分析。因此，亟需一种方法来揭示模型内部层次结构的表征机制。

Method: 开发H-probes，即一系列线性探测器，用于从模型的隐状态中提取层次结构特征，包括节点深度和成对距离；通过合成树遍历任务和全面消融实验，验证其有效性、低维性、因果作用及泛化能力；同时在真实世界任务（如数学推理）中进行对比分析。

Result: H-probes在合成任务中成功定位到包含层次结构的低维子空间，该子空间对任务性能有显著影响且具有良好的泛化能力；在真实层次任务中也检测到弱化的但可辨识的层次结构。

Conclusion: 大语言模型不仅在表层（语法与概念）上表示层次结构，还在深层抽象（如推理过程）中构建并利用层次化表征，这为理解模型的内在推理机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: Representing and navigating hierarchy is a fundamental primitive of reasoning. Large language models have demonstrated proficiency in a wide variety of tasks requiring hierarchical reasoning, but there exists limited analysis on how the models geometrically represent the necessary latent constructions for such thinking. To this end, we develop \textit{H-probes}, a collection of linear probes that extract hierarchical structure, specifically depth and pairwise distance, from latent representations. In synthetic tree traversal tasks, the H-probes robustly find the subspaces containing hierarchical structure necessary to complete the tasks; furthermore, in comprehensive ablation experiments, we show that these hierarchy-containing subspaces are low-dimensional, causally important for high task performance, and generalize within- and out-of-domain. Furthermore, we find analogous, though weaker, hierarchical structure in real-world hierarchical contexts such as mathematical reasoning traces. These results demonstrate that models represent hierarchy not only at the level of syntax and concepts, but at deeper levels of abstraction -- including the reasoning process itself.

</details>


### [59] [Model Organisms Are Leaky: Perplexity Differencing Often Reveals Finetuning Objectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00994)
*Mohammed Abu Baker,Luca Baroni,Dan Wilhelm*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于困惑度的简单方法，通过分析微调模型在随机前缀下的生成结果，识别其微调目标。该方法利用模型过度泛化微调行为的特性，通过比较微调模型与参考模型的困惑度差异，排序并筛选出最可能揭示微调目标的文本完成。实验覆盖76个不同规模（0.5到700亿参数）的模型，包括后门模型、合成文档微调模型、对抗训练中隐藏有害行为的模型以及表现出新兴对齐偏差的模型。结果表明，该方法在绝大多数情况下能有效定位微调目标，尤其对合成文档微调或精确生成特定短语的模型尤为敏感。此外，即使没有原始预训练检查点，使用来自不同模型家族的可信参考模型也能取得良好效果。由于仅需访问下一词元概率，该方法适用于暴露词元对数概率的API受保护模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微调可能显著改变大语言模型的行为，甚至引入有害或不安全行为。目前缺乏有效手段来识别这些微调目标，限制了对潜在风险的研究和评估。因此需要一种无需依赖模型内部结构或先验假设的方法，以系统性地探测微调引入的行为模式。

Method: 1. 使用来自通用语料库的短随机前缀生成多样化的文本补全；2. 计算微调模型与参考模型在每条补全上的困惑度差值（即困惑度差距）；3. 按照困惑度差距降序排列补全结果；4. 分析排名靠前的补全内容，识别其是否揭示了微调目标。该方法不依赖模型内部结构，也不需要预先知道具体行为类型。

Result: 在76个测试模型中，该方法在绝大多数情况下成功将揭示微调目标的补全排在前列。特别是针对通过合成文档微调或要求精确生成特定短语的模型，表现尤为突出。即使无法获取原始预训练模型，使用来自不同模型家族的可信参考模型仍可有效替代。该方法兼容仅提供词元对数概率的API接口模型，具备实际部署潜力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于困惑度差距的分析方法是一种高效、无需先验知识且可广泛适用的工具，能够有效揭示大语言模型微调过程中引入的目标行为，为模型安全评估和风险检测提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Finetuning can significantly modify the behavior of large language models, including introducing harmful or unsafe behaviors. To study these risks, researchers develop model organisms: models finetuned to exhibit specific known behaviors for controlled experimentation. Identifying these behaviors remains challenging. We show that a simple perplexity-based method can surface finetuning objectives from model organisms by leveraging their tendency to overgeneralize their finetuned behaviors beyond the intended context. First, we generate diverse completions from the finetuned model using short random prefills drawn from general corpora. Second, we rank completions by decreasing perplexity gap between reference and finetuned models. The top-ranked completions often reveal the finetuning objectives, without requiring model internals or prior assumptions about the behavior. We evaluate this on a diverse set of model organisms (N=76, 0.5 to 70B parameters), including backdoored models, models finetuned to internalize false facts via synthetic document finetuning, adversarially trained models with hidden concerning behaviors, and models exhibiting emergent misalignment. For the vast majority of model organisms tested, the method surfaces completions revealing finetuning objectives within the top-ranked results, with models trained via synthetic document finetuning or to produce exact phrases being particularly susceptible. We further show that the technique can be effective even without access to the exact pre-finetuning checkpoint: trusted reference models from different families can serve as effective substitutes. As the method requires only next-token probabilities from the finetuned model, it is compatible with API-gated models that expose token logprobs.

</details>


### [60] [Can AI Debias the News? LLM Interventions Improve Cross-Partisan Receptivity but LLMs Overestimate Their Own Effectiveness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01006)
*Faisal Feroz,Jonas R. Kunst*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在去偏党派新闻内容方面的潜力。两项预注册实验表明，对自由派新闻标题进行实质性重述（而非仅替换情感词汇）可显著提升保守派读者对新闻的信任度、完整性和参与意愿，且未引发自由派读者的反弹。然而，尽管模拟硅参与者表现出类似趋势，其反应幅度远大于人类，揭示出当前模型在心理机制理解上的不足。结论指出，基于框架而非表面语言的去偏策略有效，但模型仍缺乏评估自身干预效果所需的准确性和心理契合度，需人类监督。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 党派新闻媒体削弱跨党派信任，而大型语言模型（LLMs）提供了大规模去偏的可能性。本研究旨在检验LLM能否通过重构新闻内容提升保守派读者对自由派新闻的信任与接受度，并评估模型自我评估能力的局限性。

Method: 采用两项预注册实验：研究1测试轻微词汇去偏（用中性词替换情感化词语）；研究2实施更深层次的内容重述干预。分别在真实人类读者和LLM模拟的虚拟参与者中比较干预效果，并通过调节分析探索模型对响应人群的心理假设与实际人类心理特征之间的差异。

Result: 研究1中，词汇去偏对人类无显著影响，但在模拟参与者中有效；研究2中，实质性重述显著提升了保守派读者对新闻的信任度、完整性和参与意愿，且未引发自由派反弹。模拟参与者反应方向一致但强度更大，表明模型对人类心理响应的预测存在偏差。

Conclusion: LLM-based去偏可通过调整意识形态框架来增强跨党派接受度，但当前模型在量化准确性和心理真实性上仍不足，无法独立评估其干预效果，必须依赖人类监督。

Abstract: Partisan news media erode cross-partisan trust, but large language models (LLMs) offer a potential means of debiasing such content at scale. Across two pre-registered experiments, we tested whether LLM-generated debiasing of liberal news headlines could improve conservative readers' trust-relevant judgments. Study 1 found that subtle lexical debiasing (replacing emotive words with more moderate synonyms) had no effect on any outcome. Study 2 found that a more substantive reframing intervention significantly increased conservatives' perceived trustworthiness, completeness, and willingness to engage with liberal news headlines, without producing a backfire effect among a sample of liberals. In Study 1, the intervention produced robust effects among LLM-simulated silicon participants, whereas it had no impact on human readers. In Study 2, the intervention's effects among silicon participants aligned directionally with human responses but were significantly larger in magnitude for some outcomes. Moderation analyses revealed that the model's implicit theory of who responds to debiasing diverged from the psychological profile that actually predicted human responsiveness. These findings demonstrate that LLM-based debiasing can improve cross-partisan receptivity when targeting ideological framing rather than surface-level language, but that current models lack both the quantitative accuracy and qualitative psychological fidelity to evaluate their own interventions without human oversight.

</details>


### [61] [CLEAR: Revealing How Noise and Ambiguity Degrade Reliability in LLMs for Medicine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01011)
*Kevin H. Guo,Chao Yan,Avinash Baidya,Katherine Brown,Xiang Goa,Juming Xiong,Zhijun Yin,Bradley A. Malin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CLEAR框架揭示了医疗大模型评估中因答案空间设计、模糊性和不确定性导致的推理缺陷，发现模型在面对更多合理选项或不确定表述时更易出错，且随着模型规模增大，其谦逊性（abstention能力）反而下降，暴露了现有评估方法的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医疗大模型评估依赖简化、类似考试的基准，无法反映真实临床情境中的模糊性和不确定性，亟需更贴近现实的评估框架来检验模型的可靠性与决策能力。

Method: 提出CLEAR框架，通过系统性扰动答案选项数量、是否存在真值或弃权选项、以及选项的语义表述（如从"无以上"到"我不知道"），评估不同条件下大模型的推理表现。

Result: 1. 答案选项增多会降低模型正确识别答案和拒绝错误答案的能力；2. 当弃权表述由肯定性拒绝转向不确定性表达（如IDK）时，模型更倾向于选择错误答案；3. 模型规模越大，其在正确回答与恰当弃权之间的差距（即谦逊缺陷）越显著。

Conclusion: 标准医疗基准存在明显缺陷，单纯扩大模型规模无法解决其可靠性问题，未来评估应纳入对模糊性与不确定性处理能力的考量。

Abstract: Medical large language model (LLM) evaluations rely on simplified, exam-style benchmarks that rarely reflect the ambiguity of real-world medical inquiries. We introduce the CLinical Evaluation of Ambiguity and Reliability (CLEAR) framework, which assesses how decision-space presentation, ambiguity, and uncertainty affect LLMs' reasoning on medical benchmarks. CLEAR systematically perturbs (1) the number of plausible answer options, (2) the presence of a ground truth or abstention option, and (3) the semantic framing of answer options. Applying CLEAR on three benchmarks evaluated across 17 LLMs reveals three notable limitations of existing evaluation methods. First, increasing the number of plausible answers degrades a model's ability to identify the correct answer and abstain against incorrect ones. Second, this lack of caution intensifies as the framing of abstention shifts from assertive rejection like "None of the Above" to uncertainty admission like "I don't know" (IDK). Notably, just including IDK in the answer space increases incorrect answer selections. Lastly, we formalize the performance gap between identifying the correct answer and abstaining from incorrect ones as the humility deficit, which worsens with model scale. Our findings reveal limitations in standard medical benchmarks and underscore that scaling alone does not resolve LLM reliability issues.

</details>


### [62] [Psychologically Potent, Computationally Invisible: LLMs Generate Social-Comparison Triggers They Fail to Detect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01017)
*Hua Zhao,Jiapei Gu,Michelle Mingyue Gu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出XHS-SCoRE基准，用于检测小红书文本是否从第一人称读者视角引发向上、向下或中性社会比较；发现生成流畅性与可靠检测能力之间存在不匹配，提示词驱动的LLM分类器在识别该信号时表现不稳定，尤其对触发比较的文本有中性化倾向和模型特定方向偏差；控制实验表明，LLM生成的小红书风格内容可改变感知地位和比较相关情绪，但基于提示的检测仍脆弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检测小红书文本是否引发读者的社会比较，捕捉行为上真实但无法简化为情感的社交关系信号，揭示提示词方法在识别此类社会意义信号上的局限性。

Method: 构建XHS-SCoRE基准，采用提示式LLM分类器与监督中文编码器基线进行对比，结合控制实验分析生成内容对感知影响与检测稳定性之间的差异。

Result: 提示式LLM分类器表现出稳定但可解释的失败模式，如中性化比较触发文本和模型特定方向偏移；生成内容虽能改变感知与情绪，但其社会比较信号难以通过提示方式稳定检测。

Conclusion: XHS-SCoRE不仅提供一个读者根基的社会比较检测基准，还构建了一个诊断框架，揭示了社会有意义的关系线索在提示推理中可能部分不可见的问题。

Abstract: We introduce Xiaohongshu Social Comparison Reader Elicitation (XHS-SCoRE), a reader-grounded benchmark for detecting if a text-only Xiaohongshu (RedNote) post elicits UPWARD, DOWNWARD, or NEUTRAL/no clear social comparison from a first-person reader perspective. The task targets a socially meaningful relational signal that is behaviorally real yet not reducible to sentiment. Across prompted LLM classifiers and supervised Chinese encoder baselines, we find a consistent mismatch between generation fluency and reliable detection ability: the signal is textually learnable in-domain, but not robustly accessible to prompt-based classification. Prompted LLM classifiers exhibit stable, interpretable failure modes, especially neutralization of comparison-triggering posts and model-specific directional skew. A controlled pilot further shows that LLM-generated Xiaohongshu-style posts can shift perceived standing and comparison-related affect even when prompt-based detection of the same construct remains fragile. XHS-SCoRE contributes both a benchmark for reader-grounded comparison detection and a diagnostic framework for studying when socially meaningful relational cues remain only partially visible to prompt-based inference.

Abstract: As large language models grow increasingly capable, concerns about their safe deployment have intensified. In this work, we introduce a theoretical framework that formalizes a game between an attacker and a defender. Within this framework, we design a theoretical best-response attack strategy and show that it is closely related to many existing adversarial prompting methods. We further analyze the resulting game, characterize its equilibria, and reveal inherent advantages for the attacker. Drawing on our theoretical analysis, we also derive a provably optimal defense strategy. Empirically, we evaluate a practical instantiation of the theoretically optimal attack and observe stronger performance relative to existing adversarial prompting approaches in diverse settings encompassing different LLMs and benchmarks.

### [64] [Compared to What? Baselines and Metrics for Counterfactual Prompting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01048)
*Zihao Yang,Mosh Levy,Yoav Goldberg,Byron C. Wallace*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文指出，反事实提示（如改变单一因素并测量输出变化）在评估大语言模型偏见和思维链忠实性时存在缺陷，因为其观察到的效果可能源于文本表面形式的非目标变化，而非目标因素本身。作者提出一种新框架，通过将目标干预与改写输入（paraphrasing）的效应进行统计比较，以控制模型对一般形式变化的敏感性。实验表明，许多先前报告的模型对患者人口统计或风格线索的敏感性在考虑这种基线敏感性后不再显著；而在职业传记分类中，该框架成功检测到明显的性别偏向。此外，每样本度量比聚合度量更有效，回归分析则能独特地刻画效应方向与大小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反事实提示方法无法区分目标因素的影响与由文本表面形式变化引起的模型敏感性，导致对模型行为的误判。为解决这一问题，需建立一个能控制一般形式敏感性的基准，从而更准确地评估特定干预的真实影响。

Method: 提出一种基于统计检验的框架：将目标干预（如改变患者性别）的结果与等效改写输入（即语义不变但表达方式不同的句子）的结果进行对比，通过显著性检验判断目标干预是否产生额外影响。同时评估多种度量方式（聚合、分布、回归），以确定最有效的分析工具。

Result: 在MedQA数据集上，性别变更引发的预测翻转率（14.9%）与改写输入的翻转率（14.1%）无统计差异，说明不能归因于性别敏感性。在MedPerturb数据集上，原报告的120个测试中仅5个保持显著，其余大多不显著。而在职业传记分类任务中，框架识别出明确且显著的性别偏向。此外，每样本度量显著优于聚合度量，回归分析可有效揭示效应的方向与强度。

Conclusion: 反事实提示的有效性依赖于对模型一般形式敏感性的控制。所提出的比较框架能够更稳健地识别真实因果效应，避免虚假敏感性误判，尤其适用于检测微弱但定向的偏见。

Abstract: Counterfactual prompting (i.e., perturbing a single factor and measuring output change) is widely used to evaluate things like LLM bias and CoT faithfulness. But in this work we argue that observed effects cannot be attributed to the targeted factor without accounting for baseline ``meaning-preserving'' modifications to text that establish general model sensitivity. This is because every counterfactual edit is a compound treatment that bundles the variable of interest with incidental surface-form variation; this violates treatment variation irrelevance. We observe prediction flip rates on MedQA of 14.9% when we surgically change patient gender. However, this is statistically indistinguishable from the flip rates induced by simply paraphrasing inputs (14.1%). In this case, it would therefore be unwarranted to conclude that the LLM is especially sensitive to patient gender. To account for this and robustly measure the effects of targeted interventions, we propose a framework in which we compare (via statistical testing) differences observed under target interventions to those induced by paraphrasing inputs. We then use this framework to revisit a analysis done on the MedPerturb dataset, which reported evidence of model sensitivity to patient demographics and stylistic cues. We find that these effects largely dissipate when we account for general model sensitivity, with only 5 of 120 tests reaching statistical significance. Applying the same framework to occupational biography classification, we detect clearly significant directional gender bias, showing that the framework identifies real directional effects even when they are small. We evaluate a range of metrics -- aggregate, per-sample distributional, and regression -- and find that per-sample metrics are dramatically more powerful than aggregate metrics and regression powerfully and uniquely characterizes effect direction and magnitude.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究虽已为隐私预算分配提供基础，但缺乏对文本分解和预算分配策略组合效果的系统性评估，亟需明确如何在保持隐私保护的同时最大化文本可用性。

Method: 通过系统实验比较多种文本分块方法与ε预算分配策略的组合，分析其在差分隐私文本混淆中的表现差异。

Abstract: The goal of differentially private text obfuscation is to obfuscate, or "perturb", input texts with Differential Privacy (DP) guarantees, such that the private output texts are quantifiably indistinguishable from the originals. While perturbation at the word level is intuitive, meaningful text privatization happens on complete documents. Recent research has laid the groundwork for reasoning about privacy budget distribution, namely, how an overall $\varepsilon$ budget can be sensibly distributed among the component pieces of a text. We perform a systematic evaluation of multiple text decomposition and budget distribution techniques in the context of DP text obfuscation, testing how different methods for chunking texts can be combined with techniques for allocating $\varepsilon$ to these chunks. Our experiments reveal that such design choices are very important, as even with comparable privacy budgets, significantly different results can occur based on which methods are chosen. In this, we provide credible evidence of the feasibility of maximizing empirical trade-offs by optimizing DP obfuscation procedures.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The paper studies the local geometry of embedding clouds induced by \emph{controlled local classes of semantically close sentences}. The central question is how controlled paraphrase-like semantic variation is organized in sentence embedding space and whether this local structure can be explicitly modeled by low-degree fitted carriers.
  We introduce a local geometric modeling scheme based on affine, quadratic, and cubic fitted models. We also use a surface-based latent probing procedure that constructs synthetic latent points in a reduced local PCA space with respect to the fitted carrier. The procedure is intended as an offline method for representation-space analysis, local manifold modeling, and geometry-aware latent probing.
  Generated latent points are evaluated using criteria that measure consistency with the fitted surface, preservation of neighborhood structure, agreement with the empirical distribution, stability of Hessian-based second-order shape descriptors, and stability of fitted-model coefficients. Experiments on controlled sets of semantically close sentences show that nonlinear local models describe embedding clouds more accurately than affine models. Surface-based generation provides strong fitted-geometry fidelity, including surface consistency, Hessian-based shape consistency, and coefficient consistency.
  Downstream experiments show that geometric validity of synthetic latent points does not automatically translate into improved classification performance. The results support explicit local geometric modeling of sentence embedding space and highlight the need to distinguish geometric validity from discriminative utility. As a resource contribution, we introduce \textbf{CoPaGE-300K}, a controlled template-based dataset of semantically close sentence variants with slot-level annotations and precomputed sentence embeddings.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出对立指数以衡量标注者观点对立程度；利用文本特征建模并预测标注方差与对立水平，比较直接预测方差与从标注分布推断方差两种方法。

Result: 估计的标注方差与实际方差呈中等正相关；两种预测方法性能相当；高对立指数样本更难预测且常被低估。

Abstract: It is increasingly recognized that human annotators do not always agree, and such disagreement is inherent in many annotation tasks. However, not all instances in a given task elicit the same degree of opinion divergence. In this paper, we investigate annotation variation patterns in graded human ratings for inappropriate languages, including offensive language, hate speech, and toxic language perception. We examine whether the degree of annotation disagreement can be predicted from textual features. We further propose the Opposition Index, a metric that quantifies perspective opposition among annotators on a given item, and investigate the predictability of instances with potentially opposing human opinions. Our results show a moderate positive correlation between estimated and observed annotation variance. We find that two approaches achieve comparable performance in variance prediction: directly predicting the variance value and estimating it from predicted annotation distributions. Our results on opposition perspective prediction show that items with high opposition index values are more difficult to predict and are often underestimated by models.

### [69] [Compute Optimal Tokenization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01188)
*Tomasz Limisiewicz,Artidoro Pagnoni,Srini Iyer,Mike Lewis,Sachin Mehta,Alisa Liu,Margaret Li,Gargi Ghosh,Luke Zettlemoyer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了令牌的信息粒度（由压缩率控制，即每个令牌的平均字节数）对缩放趋势的影响。通过训练988个参数范围从50M到7B的潜在分词模型（BLT），能够设定所需的压缩率，从而在远超常用BPE分词器4.57字节/令牌的情况下研究压缩率的作用。实验发现，在计算最优配置下，模型参数数量与以字节为单位的数据量成正比，而非传统认为的以令牌数为单位。此外，最优压缩率不同于BPE获得的值，且随计算资源增加而降低。这些发现适用于潜在和子词分词，以及除英语以外的语言，为语言模型开发者选择分词方案以实现最大计算效率提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的缩放定律虽能优化数据量和语言模型规模的选择，但对数据单位（即令牌）在该关系中的影响仍研究不足。特别是，令牌的信息粒度（由压缩率决定）如何影响缩放趋势尚不明确。因此，需要系统研究压缩率对模型性能和计算效率的影响，以更准确地指导模型设计。

Method: 采用988个参数范围从50M到7B的潜在分词模型（BLT），通过调整压缩率来控制令牌的信息粒度。实验设置涵盖不同压缩率、模型大小和数据量，评估在不同计算资源配置下的模型表现，分析模型参数与数据量之间的缩放关系，并比较不同分词方式（如潜在分词与子词分词）及多种语言的表现。

Result: 在计算最优配置下，模型参数数量与数据量以字节为单位呈正比，而非以令牌数为单位。最优压缩率不同于标准BPE分词器的压缩率，且随着计算资源的增加而降低。这些结论在不同分词方法和多语言场景中均具有普遍性。

Conclusion: 信息粒度（压缩率）显著影响语言模型的缩放规律。最优的压缩率并非固定值，而是随计算能力动态变化。因此，语言模型开发应基于计算效率重新审视分词策略，优先考虑以字节为单位的数据量进行缩放优化，从而提升整体效率。

Abstract: Scaling laws enable the optimal selection of data amount and language model size, yet the impact of the data unit, the token, on this relationship remains underexplored. In this work, we systematically investigate how the information granularity of tokens, controlled by the compression rate (i.e., average bytes of text per token), affects scaling trends. We train 988 latent tokenized models (BLT) ranging from 50M to 7B parameters that enable setting the desired compression rate. This flexibility allows us to study the role of compression rate well beyond 4.57 bytes per token obtained with a popular BPE tokenizer. Our experiments reveal that in compute-optimal configurations, model parameter counts scale proportionally to data size measured in bytes, not in tokens as commonly perceived (Kaplan et al., 2020; Hoffmann et al., 2022). Furthermore, we discover that the optimal compression rate differs from the one obtained with BPE and decreases with compute. These findings generalize to both latent and subword tokenization, as well as to languages other than English, guiding language model developers on tokenization scheme selection for maximal compute efficiency.

### [70] [SRA: Span Representation Alignment for Large Language Model Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01205)

TL;DR: 本文提出SRA（Span Representation Alignment），一种基于多粒子动力系统物理视角的跨分词器知识蒸馏框架，将对齐单位从脆弱的词元升级为鲁棒的、分词器无关的文本片段。通过中心质心（CoM）建模每个片段，并结合注意力权重捕捉语义信息，同时引入几何正则化和对齐片段logit蒸馏，显著提升跨架构知识迁移效果，在多个挑战性实验中优于现有最先进方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有跨分词器知识蒸馏方法主要依赖词元级对齐，但此类策略对分词器差异敏感且易失效；本文认为在蒸馏前将词元聚合为更稳健的表示更为关键，旨在构建更具鲁棒性和语义丰富性的对齐机制。

Method: 提出SRA框架，将文本片段视为粒子集群，用注意力加权的中心质心（CoM）表征其状态，利用几何正则化保持表示空间结构，结合对齐片段logit蒸馏增强知识传递，实现分词器无关的高效对齐。

Result: 在多个跨架构知识蒸馏任务中，SRA显著优于当前最先进的CTKD方法，验证了其物理启发式设计的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: SRA通过将对齐粒度从词元提升至语义片段，并借助物理类比与注意力机制实现更稳定的知识迁移，为跨分词器知识蒸馏提供了新的范式，具有良好的通用性与性能优势。

Abstract: Cross-Tokenizer Knowledge Distillation (CTKD) enables knowledge transfer between a large language model and a smaller student, even when they employ different tokenizers. While existing approaches mainly focus on token-level alignment strategies, which are often brittle and sensitive to discrepancies between tokenizers, we argue that the method of aggregating tokens into more robust representations before distillation is of equal importance. In this paper, we introduce \textbf{SRA} (\textbf{S}pan \textbf{R}epresentation \textbf{A}lignment for Large Language Model Distillation), a novel framework that reframes CTKD through the physical lens of Multi-Particle Dynamical Systems. SRA shifts the fundamental unit of alignment from tokens to robust, tokenizer-agnostic spans. We model each span as a cluster of particles and represent its state by its Center of Mass (CoM) - an attention-weighted average that captures rich semantic information. We leverage the concept of span centers of mass with attention-derived weighting to prioritize the most salient spans. In addition, we employ a geometric regularizer to preserve the structural integrity of the representation space and introduce aligned span logit distillation to enhance knowledge transfer across models. In challenging cross-architecture distillation experiments, SRA consistently and significantly outperforms state-of-the-art CTKD baselines, validating our physically-grounded approach.

</details>


### [71] [GIFT: Guided Fine-Tuning and Transfer for Enhancing Instruction-Tuned Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01256)
*Zhiwen Ruan,Yichao Du,Jianjie Zheng,Longyue Wang,Yun Chen,Peng Li,Jinsong Su,Yang Liu,Guanhua Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GIFT是一种简单高效的框架，通过利用指令调优模型的置信度信号指导任务适应过程，实现对预训练基础模型的低秩适配器微调，并将其合并到指令调优模型中，从而在保持通用指令遵循能力的同时提升特定任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将指令调优模型视为被动目标，仅在最终合并阶段参与，缺乏对训练过程的引导。为提升任务适应效果并保持模型泛化能力，需要一种能主动利用指令模型信息的指导性策略。

Method: GIFT通过从指令调优模型中提取置信度信号，指导在预训练基础模型上进行低秩适配器的微调，随后将学习到的适配器合并到指令调优模型中，形成任务专业化模型。

Result: 在数学和知识密集型基准测试中，GIFT在多个模型家族和规模下均优于直接微调和代表性迁移基线，同时保持良好的泛化能力和有利的测试时缩放行为。

Conclusion: GIFT通过引入来自指令调优模型的指导信号，有效提升了任务适应效率与性能，是实现高效、可扩展的任务定制化语言模型的有效方法。

Abstract: A promising paradigm for adapting instruction-tuned language models is to learn task-specific updates on a pretrained base model and subsequently merge them into the instruction-tuned model. However, existing approaches typically treat the instruction-tuned model as a passive target that is only involved at the final merging stage, without guiding the training process. We propose GIFT (Guided Fine-Tuning and Transfer), a simple and efficient framework that incorporates guidance from the instruction model into task adaptation. GIFT fine-tunes a low-rank adapter on the pretrained base model using confidence signals derived from the instruction-tuned model. The learned adapter is then merged into the instruction-tuned model, yielding task-specialized models that preserve general instruction-following behavior. We evaluate GIFT on mathematical and knowledge-intensive benchmarks across multiple model families and scales. Results show that GIFT consistently outperforms direct fine-tuning and representative transfer-based baselines, while maintaining robust generalization and favorable test-time scaling behavior.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 PUPPET 框架，利用双重奖励信号（检测器输出的机器生成概率 + 任务特定评估指标）通过强化学习微调 LLM，优化生成内容的可检测性与任务表现之间的平衡。

Conclusion: PUPPET 证明了通过强化学习联合优化可检测性与任务性能是可行且高效的，为安全可控的 LLM 输出提供了一种新的解决方案。

Abstract: Detecting machine-generated text is essential for transparency and accountability when deploying large language models (LLMs). Among detection approaches, watermarking is a statistically reliable method by design -- it embeds detectable signals into LLM outputs by biasing their token distributions. However, it has been reported that watermarked LLMs often perform worse on downstream tasks. We propose PUPPET, a framework that fine-tunes an LLM via reinforcement learning to generate text that is both more detectable and better performing on downstream tasks. We use two reward functions: a detector that outputs a machine-class likelihood and an evaluator that measures a task-specific metric. Experiments on long-form QA, summarization, and essay writing show that LLMs trained with PUPPET achieve high detectability competitive with watermarking methods while outperforming them on downstream tasks. ### [77] [On Stable Long-Form Generation: Benchmarking and Mitigating Length Volatility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01357)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出VOLTBench基准测试以量化长度波动；通过注意力轨迹分析揭示导致波动的内部模式；设计GLoBo方法，在解码阶段通过逻辑值增强实现稳定生成，无需额外训练。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) excel at long-context understanding but exhibit significant limitations in long-form generation. Existing studies primarily focus on single-generation quality, generally overlooking the volatility of the output. This volatility not only leads to significant computational costs but also severely impacts the models' reliable application. To address this gap, our work unfolds in three stages: benchmarking, probing, and mitigation. We first propose the VOlatility in Long-form Text Benchmark (VOLTBench), a novel heterogeneous-task benchmark designed to systematically quantify the length volatility of long-form generation. Subsequently, by analyzing attention traces, we conduct an in-depth probe to identify several common internal patterns that cause this volatility. Finally, to mitigate long-form output volatility, we propose Stable Generation via Logits Boosting (GLoBo), a lightweight decoding-stage optimization strategy, designed to significantly enhance both the length accuracy and stability of long-form generation without additional training. Extensive experiments on VOLTBench provide the first systematic confirmation of severe long-form output instability in mainstream models and validate that our proposed method successfully improves the mean output length of the base model by 148% and reduces the length volatility by 69%, while maintaining high generation quality.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: EPIC 将文本演示替换为对应的连续嵌入，利用对比学习促使模型对语义相关的文本对进行对齐，并使模型学会将演示嵌入作为上下文提示的一部分进行理解。

Result: EPIC 在 MTEB 基准上超越仅使用公开检索数据训练的前沿模型，实现新的最先进性能；无论是否使用上下文提示，均表现出色。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have been widely explored for embedding generation. While recent studies show that in-context learning (ICL) effectively enhances the representational capability of LLMs by prepending a few task-related demonstrations, it causes substantial token overhead due to the increased sequence length. In this work, we propose EPIC, a novel embedding-based in-context prompt training strategy that leverages ICL to generate high-quality embeddings while reducing computational burden during both training and inference. Consequently, EPIC-trained models achieve excellent embedding performance both with or without in-context prompts at inference time. *Jinyuan Feng,Xin Yu,Yiqun Chen,Xiaochi Wei,Yan Gao,Yi Wu,Yao Hu,Zhiqiang Pu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出FoCore和FoCore_A两种解码策略，利用高信息密度（HD）token提升扩散语言模型的生成质量与效率。FoCore通过自对比机制临时遮蔽HD token作为负样本引导生成；FoCore_A在检测到HD token收敛后并行解码局部稳定候选，显著加速。实验表明，在数学、代码和逻辑推理任务上均有效提升性能，如HumanEval上pass@1从39.02提升至42.68，延迟降低58.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有解码策略未能充分利用扩散语言模型在全局上下文建模上的优势，存在局部偏好问题，忽视上下文中的信息密度异质性，导致生成质量下降。

Method: 系统研究高信息密度（HD）token，发现其对生成质量有显著影响且具有早期收敛特性；提出训练无关的FoCore策略，通过自对比方式利用HD token引导生成；进一步设计FoCore_A，基于HD token收敛检测实现并行解码以加速。

Result: 在数学、代码和逻辑推理基准测试中，FoCore显著提升生成质量，FoCore_A大幅减少解码步数（2.07倍）和每样本延迟（-58.4%），在LLaDA和Dream模型上均表现优异。

Conclusion: HD token在扩散语言模型中具有关键作用，利用其早期收敛特性的解码策略能有效提升生成质量与效率，所提出的FoCore及FoCore_A为高效、高质量文本生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: The iterative denoising paradigm of Diffusion Large Language Models (DLMs) endows them with a distinct advantage in global context modeling. However, current decoding strategies fail to leverage this capability, typically exhibiting a local preference that overlooks the heterogeneous information density within the context, ultimately degrading generation quality. To address this limitation, we systematically investigate high-information-density (HD) tokens and present two key findings: (1) explicitly conditioning on HD tokens substantially improves output quality; and (2) HD tokens exhibit an early-decoding tendency, converging earlier than surrounding tokens. Motivated by these findings, we propose Focus on the Core \textbf{(FoCore)}, a training-free decoding strategy that utilizes HD tokens in a self-contrast manner, wherein HD tokens are temporarily remasked as negative samples, to guide generation. We further introduce FoCore\_Accelerate \textbf{(FoCore\_A)}, an efficient variant that, upon detecting HD token convergence, performs parallel decoding over stable candidates within a local context window, substantially accelerating generation. Extensive experiments on math, code and logical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that FoCore consistently improves generation quality and efficiency across both LLaDA and Dream backbones. For instance, on HumanEval, FoCore improves pass@1 from 39.02 to 42.68 over standard Classifier-Free Guidance, while FoCore-A reduces the number of decoding steps by 2.07x and per-sample latency from 20.76s to 8.64s (-58.4\%).

</details>


### [80] [MTA: Multi-Granular Trajectory Alignment for Large Language Model Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01374)
*Pham Khanh Chi,Quoc Phong Dao,Thuat Nguyen,Linh Ngo Van,Trung Le,Thanh Hong Nguyen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出多粒度轨迹对齐（MTA）框架，通过在不同层别对齐教师与学生模型的表示，以更好地捕捉深层语义结构。低层进行词级对齐以保留词汇信息，高层则对短语级片段（如名词短语、动词短语）进行对齐以捕获组合语义。采用动态结构对齐损失匹配各层内语义单元间的相对几何关系，并结合隐藏表示对齐损失。实验表明MTA在标准基准上优于现有方法，且消融实验证明各组件的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识蒸馏方法通常在固定层或词级别对齐表示，忽略了表示随深度演变的过程，导致学生模型难以有效学习教师模型内部的语义关系结构，限制了知识迁移效果。

Method: 提出多粒度轨迹对齐（MTA）框架，采用分层自适应策略：低层进行词级对齐，高层对短语级跨度进行对齐；引入动态结构对齐损失以匹配各层内语义单元之间的相对几何关系，并结合隐藏表示对齐损失直接对齐特定层。

Result: MTA在多个标准基准测试中持续优于现有先进基线方法；消融实验验证了动态结构对齐损失和隐藏表示对齐损失各自组件的有效性。

Conclusion: MTA通过分层自适应地对齐教师与学生模型的表示轨迹，有效提升了知识蒸馏过程中对深层语义结构的捕捉能力，显著增强了知识迁移效果。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation is a key technique for compressing large language models (LLMs), but most existing methods align representations at fixed layers or token-level outputs, ignoring how representations evolve across depth. As a result, the student is only weakly guided to capture the teacher's internal relational structure during distillation, which limits knowledge transfer. To address this limitation, we propose Multi-Granular Trajectory Alignment (MTA), a framework that aligns teacher and student representations along their layer-wise transformation trajectory. MTA adopts a layer-adaptive strategy: lower layers are aligned at the word level to preserve lexical information, while higher layers operate on phrase-level spans (e.g., noun and verb phrases) to capture compositional semantics. We instantiate this idea through a Dynamic Structural Alignment loss that matches the relative geometry among semantic units within each layer. This design is motivated by empirical findings that Transformer representations become increasingly abstract with depth, and is also consistent with linguistic views in which higher-level meaning emerges through the composition of lower-level lexical units. We further incorporate a Hidden Representation Alignment loss to directly align selected teacher-student layers. Experiments show that MTA consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on standard benchmarks, with ablations confirming the contribution of each component.

</details>


### [81] [A framework for analyzing concept representations in neural models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01381)
*Burin Naowarat,Hao Tang,Sharon Goldwater*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一框架，用于研究神经模型中概念子空间的两个属性：包含性（containment）和解耦性（disentanglement）。实验表明，概念子空间并非唯一确定，不同估计器对这两个属性有显著影响。LEACE方法在两项测试中表现良好，但在未见数据上泛化能力不足；在HuBERT语音表示中，音素信息既被包含又与说话人信息解耦，而说话人信息虽解耦但难以在紧凑子空间中被包含。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解神经模型如何表征人类可解释的概念极具挑战性。现有工作从探测和概念擦除等角度研究线性概念子空间，但缺乏统一框架来系统评估其性质。

Method: 提出一个基于包含性和解耦性的统一分析框架，比较五种来自不同领域的概念子空间估计器，并在文本和语音模型上进行实验验证。

Result: 1. 估计器的选择显著影响概念子空间的包含性和解耦性；2. 当前最先进的概念擦除方法LEACE在两项测试中表现良好，但泛化能力有限；3. 在HuBERT语音表示中，音素信息具有良好的包含性和解耦性，而说话人信息虽解耦但难以被紧凑地包含。

Conclusion: 概念子空间的性质受估计方法影响显著，且其唯一性需重新审视。未来工作应关注提升模型在未见数据上的泛化能力，并探索更有效的子空间表示与分离策略。

Abstract: Understanding how neural models represent human-interpretable concepts is challenging. Prior work has explored linear concept subspaces from diverse perspectives, such as probing and concept erasure. We introduce a unified framework to study these subspaces along two axes: \textit{containment}, which tests if a concept is fully represented in a subspace but not outside it, and \textit{disentanglement}, which tests for isolation from other concepts. In experiments on both text and speech models, we first highlight that concept subspaces may not be uniquely determined, and discuss the implications for concept subspace analysis. Then, we compare properties of concept subspaces estimated using five estimators, proposed in different communities. We find that (1) the choice of estimator impacts the containment and disentanglement properties; (2) the state-of-the-art concept erasure method, LEACE, performs well on both testing axes, but still struggles to generalize to unseen data; and (3) in HuBERT speech representations, phone information is both contained and disentangled from speaker information, while speaker information is hard to contain in a compact subspace, despite being disentangled from phones.

Method: 提出Verbal-R3框架，包含生成器（Generator）和语义重排序器（Verbal Reranker），结合迭代检索与推理，并利用语义注释与相关性引导的测试时扩展优化推理路径。

Abstract: The conventional Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) paradigm of injecting raw retrieved texts into the Large Language Model (LLM)'s context often results in suboptimal integration of retrieved information. This paper proposes to bridge retrieval results and the LLM's reasoning ability through Verbal Annotations, analytic narratives that explicitly articulate the logical connection between a search query and retrieved contexts. Our empirical investigation reveals the potential of Verbal Annotations to substantially enhance the LLM's ability to generate accurate, contextually-grounded responses. Motivated by this finding, we introduce Verbal-R3, a novel agentic RAG framework that consists of a Generator and a Verbal Reranker. The Generator performs iterative retrieval and reasoning, while the Verbal Reranker returns relevance scores and Verbal Annotations to guide the reasoning and answering process of the Generator. The inference process of Verbal-R3 is further refined through relevance-guided test-time scaling, which efficiently allocates test-time compute for effective trajectory expansion. Verbal-R3 achieves state-of-the-art performance on complex Question Answering benchmarks, validating the effectiveness of the proposed framework.

### [83] [Injecting Distributional Awareness into MLLMs via Reinforcement Learning for Deep Imbalanced Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01402)
*Yao Du,Shanshan Li,Xiaomeng Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于组相对策略优化的分布感知强化学习框架，以解决多模态大语言模型在长尾目标分布下的数值回归问题。现有方法因样本内监督和点对点回归奖励导致学习偏向高密度区域，引发回归均值偏差和尾部性能差的问题。本文通过引入基于一致性相关系数的批级比较监督，实现预测与真实分布间相关性、尺度和均值的对齐，无需修改模型架构，可在多种长尾回归基准上一致提升性能，尤其在中等和少样本场景下表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型在长尾目标分布下的数值回归任务中表现不佳，现有训练范式（如词元级监督微调和点对点回归奖励）倾向于聚焦高密度区域，导致回归均值偏差和尾部性能差，缺乏跨样本关系监督是关键瓶颈。

Method: 提出一种分布感知的强化学习框架，基于组相对策略优化，利用一致性相关系数设计批级比较奖励，引导模型学习预测分布与真实分布之间的相关性、尺度和均值对齐。该方法为即插即用型，无需改变模型结构。

Result: 在统一的长尾回归基准测试中，该方法显著优于监督微调和现有多模态大语言模型回归方法，在中等和少样本设置下取得尤为显著的提升。

Conclusion: 缺乏跨样本关系监督是当前多模态大语言模型在长尾回归任务中表现不佳的关键原因。通过引入基于一致性相关系数的批级比较监督，所提出的分布感知强化学习框架有效提升了模型对尾部样本的建模能力，具有良好的泛化性和实用性。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) struggle with numerical regression under long-tailed target distributions. Token-level supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and point-wise regression rewards bias learning toward high-density regions, leading to regression-to-the-mean behavior and poor tail performance. We identify the lack of cross-sample relational supervision as a key limitation of existing MLLM training paradigms. To address it, we propose a distribution-aware reinforcement learning framework based on Group Relative Policy Optimization, which introduces batch-level comparison-based supervision via the Concordance Correlation Coefficient-based reward to align predicted and ground-truth distributions in terms of correlation, scale, and mean. The framework is plug-and-play, requiring no architectural modification. Experiments on a unified suite of long-tailed regression benchmarks show consistent improvements over SFT and existing MLLM regression methods, with particularly strong gains in medium- and few-shot regimes.

Abstract: Evaluating large language models (LLMs) for medical applications remains challenging due to benchmark saturation, limited data accessibility, and insufficient coverage of relevant tasks. Existing suites have either saturated, heavily depend on restricted datasets, or lack comprehensive model coverage. We introduce Medmarks, a fully open-source evaluation suite with 30 benchmarks spanning question answering, information extraction, medical calculations, and open-ended clinical reasoning. We perform a systematic evaluation of 61 models across 71 configurations using verifiable metrics and LLM-as-a-Judge. Our results show that frontier reasoning models (Gemini 3 Pro Preview, GPT-5.1, & GPT-5.2) achieve the highest performance across both benchmarks, most frontier proprietary models are significantly more token efficient than open-weight alternatives, medically fine-tuned models outperform their generalist counterparts, and that models are susceptible to answer-order bias (particularly smaller models and Grok 4). A subset of our evals (Medmarks-T) can be directly used as reinforcement learning environments to post-train LLMs for medical reasoning. Code is available at https://github.com/MedARC-AI/Medmarks

### [86] [Auditing demographic bias in AI-based emergency police dispatch: a cross-lingual evaluation of eleven large language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01451)
*William Guey,Wei Zhang,Pierrick Bougault,Yi Wang,Bertan Ucar,Vitor D. de Moura,José O. Gomes*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种跨语言审计框架，评估大语言模型在紧急呼叫分级系统中的种族、性别和宗教外观等人口统计偏差。通过19,800个模型输出分析发现，在事件严重性模糊时存在系统性偏差，且偏差程度随不同人口维度变化，其中宗教外观偏差最大；值得注意的是，性别偏差在中文中被放大，而种族偏差在英文中更显著，揭示了跨语言不对称性。此外，某些情况下偏差方向相反，挑战了简单的刻板印象放大理论。研究强调偏差是模型、语境模糊性和语言交互作用的结果，并提供了可扩展的审计工具以支持实际部署前的模型评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型正被应用于高风险公共安全系统，但其在人口统计公平性方面的表现尚未充分检验，亟需建立可操作的评估框架来识别和缓解潜在偏见。

Method: 将警察优先调度系统转化为五级有序分类任务，采用控制的最小对偶设计，分离出人口统计线索的影响；覆盖11个前沿模型、15组场景、3个人口类别（宗教外观、性别、种族）及两种语言（英语与中文），系统评估模型输出。

Result: 当事件严重性不明确时，模型表现出系统性人口统计偏差，其中宗教外观偏差最大，其次为性别和种族；跨语言分析显示性别偏差在中文中更严重，种族偏差在英文中更突出，且部分场景出现反向偏差，表明偏差机制复杂且非单一刻板印象放大。

Conclusion: LLM在应急调度中的偏差并非模型固有属性，而是由人口信号、上下文模糊性和语言共同决定的动态交互结果。研究提出的审计框架可为部署机构提供针对本地场景的模型评估能力，推动更公平、可信赖的AI应用。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly being integrated into high-stakes public safety systems, including emergency call triage and dispatch decision support, yet their demographic fairness in this context remains largely untested. Here we introduce a cross-lingual audit framework that operationalizes the Police Priority Dispatch System as a five-level ordinal classification task and applies a controlled minimal-pair design to isolate the effect of demographic cues. Across 19,800 model outputs spanning 11 frontier models, 15 scenario pairs, three demographic categories (religious appearance, gender, and race), and two languages (English and Mandarin Chinese), we find that demographic bias emerges systematically when incident severity is ambiguous but largely disappears when the operational priority is clearly determined by call content. Bias magnitude varies by demographic axis, with the largest effects observed for religious appearance, followed by gender and race. Critically, bias does not transfer consistently across languages: gender bias is substantially amplified in Mandarin Chinese, whereas race bias is more pronounced in English, revealing cross-lingual asymmetries that aggregate analyses obscure. In several scenarios, demographic cues produce counter-directional effects, challenging simple stereotype-amplification accounts of model behavior. These findings suggest that bias in LLM-based dispatch is not a fixed property of models alone, but arises from the interaction between demographic signals, contextual ambiguity, and language. Beyond these empirical results, the proposed framework provides a scalable audit infrastructure that enables deploying agencies to evaluate candidate models on jurisdiction-relevant scenarios prior to real-world adoption.

</details>


### [87] [ReMedi: Reasoner for Medical Clinical Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01474)
*Yushi Cao,Yiming Chen,Hongchao Jiang,Hung-yi Lee,Robby T. Tan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ReMedi 是一种用于提升电子健康记录（EHR）临床结果预测的框架，通过生成带有理由的答案对，并利用真实结果作为提示来增强模型推理能力。该方法通过重构复杂临床问题的样本，将真实结果融入偏好数据构建循环，从而在微调和偏好调整中提升模型性能。实验表明，在多个EHR预测任务上，ReMedi相较于现有最先进方法在F1分数上最高提升19.9%，显著提升了临床预测效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大语言模型（LLM）的临床预测方法主要依赖模型内部对上下文信息的理解，而忽视了如何有效利用真实临床结果来指导推理过程。由于患者数据复杂且异质性强，如何提升模型对复杂临床问题的推理能力成为关键挑战。因此，需要一种机制来增强模型从EHR中提取有意义推理路径的能力。

Method: ReMedi 采用挑战性样本再生机制，以真实答案为提示生成多种理由-答案对；这些生成的配对被用于进一步的微调和偏好训练。通过将真实临床结局嵌入偏好数据构建流程，模型能够学习更准确、可解释的推理逻辑，从而提高预测准确性。

Result: 在多个EHR预测任务上的实验结果显示，ReMedi 在 F1 分数上相比当前最先进的基线方法平均提升超过 10%，最高达 19.9%。这表明该框架在真实世界临床预测中具有显著优势。

Conclusion: ReMedi 通过引入真实临床结果引导的推理生成与偏好训练机制，有效提升了大语言模型在复杂临床预测任务中的表现，为未来医疗AI系统提供了可解释、高性能的解决方案。

Abstract: Predicting future clinical outcomes from electronic health records (EHR) remains challenging due to the complexity and heterogeneity of patient data. LLMs have shown strong potential for such predictive tasks, yet existing approaches mainly focus on enhancing medical knowledge through distillation or RAG while relying on the model's internal ability to interpret contextual information. In this work, we present ReMedi (Reasoner for Medical Clinical Prediction), a framework for improving clinical outcome prediction from EHR. ReMedi generates rationale-answer pairs using a challenging sample regeneration mechanism for complex clinical questions, which leverages ground-truth answers as hints to enhance reasoning for further fine-tuning and preference tuning. ReMedi integrates ground-truth outcome guidance into the preference data construction loop, regenerating rationale-answer variants. By tuning on these rationale-answer pairs, the model improves its predictive performance. Experiments on multiple EHR prediction tasks demonstrate substantial gains of up to 19.9 percent over state-of-the-art baselines in terms of F1 score, underscoring ReMedi's effectiveness in real-world clinical prediction.

### [88] [FT-RAG: A Fine-grained Retrieval-Augmented Generation Framework for Complex Table Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01495)
*Zebin Guo,Weidong Geng,Ruichen Mao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出FT-RAG，一种针对结构化表格数据的细粒度检索增强生成框架，通过将表格分解为语义单元构建结构化图，并结合结构邻域扩展与多模态融合提升检索与生成性能。同时引入Multi-Table-RAG-Lib基准数据集以应对领域数据稀缺问题。实验表明，FT-RAG在表级和单元级命中率上分别提升23.5%和59.2%，生成准确率提升62.2%，显著优于现有方法，验证了其在混合模态文档复杂推理中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RAG系统在处理结构化表格数据时表现不佳，主要受限于粗粒度检索和对表格语义理解不足。因此需要更精细的表格理解与检索机制以提升事实性生成能力。

Method: FT-RAG将表格分解为细粒度语义单元，构建结构化图；采用结构邻域扩展机制发现语义关联实体，并通过多模态融合整合检索结果上下文。此外，构建了Multi-Table-RAG-Lib基准数据集以支持复杂推理任务。

Result: FT-RAG在表级和细胞级命中率上分别提升23.5%和59.2%，生成任务的精确值准确率召回率提高62.2%，显著超越现有基线模型，在纯表格与图文混合场景下均实现最优表现。

Conclusion: FT-RAG通过细粒度知识关联与多模态融合，有效提升了大语言模型在结构化表格数据上的推理与生成能力，建立了混合模态文档复杂推理的新基准。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) enhances Large Language Models (LLMs) by grounding responses in external knowledge during inference. However, conventiona RAG systems under-perform on structured tabular data, largely due to coarse retrieval granularity and insufficient table semantic comprehension. To address these limitations, we introduce FT-RAG, a fine-grained framework that employs knowledge association by decomposing tables into entry-level semantic units to construct a structured graph. FT-RAG employs a structural neighbor expansion mechanism to find semantically connected entities during graph retrieval, followed by multi-modal fusion to consolidate the context of table retrieval results. Further, to address the scarcity of specialized datasets in this domain, we introduce Multi-Table-RAG-Lib, a benchmark comprising 9870 QA pairs with high complexity and difficulty, curated to demand multi-table integration and text-table information fusion for reasoning. FT-RAG surpasses top-performing baselines across all metrics, achieving a 23.5\% and 59.2\% improvement in table-level and cell-level Hit Rates, respectively. Generation performance also sees a remarkable 62.2\% increase in exact value accuracy recall. These metrics verify the framework's effectiveness in factual grounding across both pure tabular and heterogeneous table-text contexts. Therefore, our method establishes a new state-of-the-art performance for complex reasoning over mixed-modality documents.

### [89] [The grip of grammar on meaning uncertainty: cross-linguistic evidence, neural correlates, and clinical relevance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01537)
*Rui He,Claudio Palominos,Samuele Vallisa,Ni Yang,Han Zhang,Miguel Ángel Santos Santos,Neguine Rezaii,Sergi Valero,Yonghua Huang,Huan Li,Hong Jiang,Yongjun Peng,Maria Francisca Alonso-Sánchez,Frederike Stein,Tilo Kircher,Philipp Homan,Iris Sommer,Lena Palaniyappan,Wolfram Hinzen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出语法通过跨语言压缩意义不确定性来促进语言理解，这种压缩体现在大脑活动中，并在语言障碍中被选择性破坏。通过比较词汇频率带来的非上下文意外度与语法敏感模型产生的上下文意外度，发现上下文意外度显著降低了基于频率的意外度，且该降低程度与词序反转的意外度成本密切相关，同时与更丰富、非冗余的词汇组织（由更复杂的最优依存结构支持）成正比。功能性磁共振成像（fMRI）显示，意外度及其减少量可解释理解和产生过程中的脑区活动，且在失语症、痴呆和精神分裂症中显著减弱，而在非语言主导缺陷的疾病中仍保持完整。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言中孤立词汇的意义具有内在不确定性，而这种不确定性在语境中得到缓解。本研究旨在揭示语法如何跨语言压缩意义不确定性，进而理解语言处理的基本原则、神经基础及语言障碍中的异常机制。

Method: 通过计算非上下文意外度（基于词汇频率）与上下文意外度（基于语法敏感模型）之间的相对差异来量化语法对意义不确定性的压缩作用。分析了来自20种语言的叙事数据，评估上下文意外度对频率意外度的降低程度，并结合词序反转的意外度成本和依存结构复杂性进行验证。同时采用fMRI研究语言理解与产出过程中的脑活动模式，对比健康个体与语言障碍患者（如失语症、痴呆、精神分裂症）的差异。

Result: 在20种语言的叙事数据中，上下文意外度显著低于频率基础上的意外度，其减少量与词序反转的意外度成本高度相关，并随更复杂的依存结构和非冗余词汇的使用而增加。fMRI结果显示，意外度及其减少量能够有效解释语言理解和产生过程中重叠但不同的脑区活动。在失语症、痴呆和精神分裂症患者中，不确定性减少效应显著减弱，而在非语言主导障碍中则保持正常。

Conclusion: 语法通过压缩意义不确定性，是语言处理的核心机制之一，不仅反映在跨语言的结构规律中，也体现于大脑活动模式，并在多种语言障碍中被选择性破坏。这一发现为理解语言的本质、其神经基础以及病理状态提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: Isolated word meanings are inherently uncertain. This uncertainty reduces when they are combined and anchored in context. We propose that grammar compresses meaning uncertainty cross-linguistically, which is reflected in brain and selectively disrupted in disorders. Compression was operationalized as the relative difference between non-contextual surprisal estimated from lexical frequency, and contextual surprisal from grammar-sensitive models. In narratives from 20 languages, contextual surprisal reduced frequency-based surprisal. This reduction closely tracked the surprisal cost of reversing word order, and scaled with richer, non-redundant lexis as organized by more complex but optimal dependency structure. During fMRI, surprisal and its reduction explained BOLD activity for comprehension and production in overlapping but distinct regions. Uncertainty reduction was significantly attenuated in aphasia, dementia, and schizophrenia, but remained intact where primary deficit is not language. These findings position uncertainty reduction via grammar as a foundational concept that illuminates principles, brain basis, and disruptions of language.

</details>


### [90] [Automated Interpretability and Feature Discovery in Language Models with Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01555)
*Arnau Marin-Llobet,Javier Ferrando*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一个自主的多智能体框架，用于大语言模型的机制可解释性，自动化地发现和解释内部特征。该框架包含两个耦合循环：解释优化（智能体提出竞争性假设并通过靶向提示控制与多指标评估进行迭代测试）和特征发现（智能体生成提示集，构建激活空间中的k近邻图，并通过统计可分离性和语义一致性标准检索候选特征）。在Gemma-2系列模型及权重稀疏Transformer中的MLP神经元上，该方法优于一次性自动解释，发现了语言特异性和安全相关特征，并生成可审计的解释轨迹，表明基于智能体的实证循环能产生更清晰、更可证伪的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型的可解释性方法多为一次性标注，缺乏迭代优化与验证机制，难以发现深层、复杂且具有实际意义的内部特征。因此需要一种自动化、可迭代、可验证的机制来提升解释的深度与可信度。

Method: 采用双循环多智能体系统：解释优化循环中，智能体提出多个竞争假设，通过靶向提示控制与多维度评估进行迭代验证；特征发现循环中，智能体生成提示集，构建激活空间的k近邻图，利用统计可分离性与语义一致性筛选候选特征。

Result: 在Gemma-2系列模型和权重稀疏变压器的MLP神经元上，该框架显著优于传统的一次性自动解释方法；成功识别出语言特异性与安全相关的特征；生成了可审计的解释过程轨迹，增强了解释的透明性与可验证性。

Conclusion: 基于智能体的双循环实证机制能够实现更精确、可验证、可审计的模型解释，推动了大语言模型可解释性从静态标签向动态、可迭代研究范式的转变。

Abstract: We introduce an autonomous multiagent framework for mechanistic interpretability that automates both explaining and finding internal features in large language models. The system runs two coupled loops: (1) explanation refinement, where an agent proposes competing hypotheses and iteratively tests them with targeted prompt controls and a multi-metric evaluation; and (2) feature discovery, where an agent generates prompt sets, constructs a k-nearest-neighbor graph in activation space, and retrieves candidate features using statistical separability and semantic coherence criteria. On Gemma-2 family models and MLP neurons in weight-sparse transformers, our agent improves over one-shot auto-interpretations, discovers language-specific and safety-relevant features, and produces auditable explanation traces, showing that agent-driven empirical loops yield sharper and more falsifiable explanations than one-shot labels.

Abstract: This paper describes the system submitted by team \textbf{Archaeology} to SemEval-2026 Task~13 on AI-generated code detection. The shared task consists of three subtasks; we participate in Subtask-A (binary classification: human-written vs.\ AI-generated code) and Subtask-B (11-class attribution of the generating model). Starting from a TF-IDF and Logistic Regression baseline, we fine-tune four pre-trained code models (CodeBERT, GraphCodeBERT, UniXcoder, and CodeT5+) with separate strategies for each subtask. For Subtask-A, we use leave-one-language-out cross-validation, code augmentation, chunked inference with trimmed-mean aggregation, and threshold calibration on a difficult dataset. For Subtask-B, we use sandwich token packing, class-balanced loss, and multi-seed ensembling with test-time augmentation. ### [92] [Prosa: Rubric-Based Evaluation of LLMs on Real User Chats in Brazilian Portuguese](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01630)
*Roseval Malaquias Junior,Giovana Kerche Bonás,Thales Sales Almeida,Hugo Abonizio,Thiago Laitz,Ramon Pires,Marcos Piau,Celio Larcher,Rodrigo Nogueira*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于二元评分标准并结合多评委过滤的评分方法（Prosa），以减少大语言模型作为评判者时因模型偏见导致的评分敏感性。实验表明，该方法在巴西葡萄牙语对话数据集上显著提升了评分一致性与区分度，三名来自不同模型家族的评委在过滤后对16个模型的排名完全一致，而传统整体评分仅达成7个一致。此外，该方法使相邻模型间平均得分差距扩大47%，且评估成本仅为约$2.1。研究开源了基准数据集和过滤代码，支持未来评估的可复现性与通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型作为评判者的整体评分方法对所选模型存在敏感性，容易受评判模型自身偏见影响，导致评分结果不可靠。因此需要一种更稳定、可复现且具有强区分能力的评估方法。

Method: 引入基于二元评分标准的多评委过滤机制，通过多个独立评委对评分标准进行验证与筛选，消除单个模型偏见的影响；同时构建首个真实用户多轮巴西葡萄牙语对话基准（Prosa），用于评估模型表现。

Result: 在Prosa基准上，使用过滤后的二元评分标准，三位评委对16个模型的排名达成完全一致；而传统整体评分仅在7个模型上达成一致。同时，相邻模型间的平均得分差距提升47%，显著增强了评估的区分能力。模型评估成本约为$2.1（使用Gemini 3 Flash）。

Conclusion: 评分过程的结构化分解（即使用二元评分与多评委过滤）比所用评判模型本身更为关键，能有效降低偏见影响，提升评估的稳定性与可靠性。该方法具备良好的可迁移性，适用于其他开放性任务的评估。

Abstract: Rankings produced by holistic LLM-as-a-judge scoring are sensitive to the bias of the chosen judge model. We show that switching to binary rubric scoring with multi-judge filtering removes this sensitivity: decomposing the judgement matters more than the judge model itself. To support this claim, we introduce Prosa, the first real user multi-turn Brazilian Portuguese chat benchmark: 1,000 WildChat conversations scored by three judges from three model families on 16 models. Under filtered rubric scoring the three judges agree on every one of the 16 ranks, whereas under holistic scoring they agree on only 7 of 16. Additionally, the rubric filtering pipeline increases the average score gap between neighbouring models by 47%, thereby improving Prosa's discriminative power. Evaluating a new model on Prosa costs approximately $2.1 when using Gemini 3 Flash as the judge. We release the benchmark and the filtering code to ensure that future models can be assessed under identical conditions. These artifacts also make our rubric-based scoring method reusable beyond Prosa, supporting other open-ended evaluation settings.

</details>


### [93] [Beyond Perplexity: Character Distribution Signatures and the MDTA Benchmark for AI Text Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01647)
*Priyadarshan Narayanasamy,Swastik Agrawal,Klint Faber,Fardina Fathmiul Alam*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于字符分布特征的无训练AI文本检测方法，通过构建MDTA基准数据集并引入LD-Score，在多个领域和对抗策略下验证了其有效性，尤其在专业领域表现突出，且与传统困惑度方法相关性低，可显著提升现有检测模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
