Abstract: Learning constraint-satisfying policies from offline data without risky online interaction is crucial for safety-critical decision making. Conventional methods typically learn cost value functions from abundant unsafe samples to define safety boundaries and penalize violations. However, in high-stakes scenarios, risky trial-and-error is infeasible, yielding datasets with few or no unsafe samples. Under this limitation, existing approaches often treat all data as uniformly safe, overlooking safe-but-infeasible states - states that currently satisfy constraints but inevitably violate them within a few steps - leading to deployment failures. Drawing inspiration from the concept of knowledge-data integration, we leverage large language models (LLMs) to incorporate natural language knowledge into the policy to address this challenge. Specifically, we propose PROCO, a model-based offline safe reinforcement learning (RL) framework tailored to datasets largely free of violations. PROCO first learns a dynamics model from offline data and constructs a conservative cost function by grounding natural-language knowledge of unsafe states in LLMs, enabling risk estimation even without observed violations. Using the cost function and learned model, PROCO performs model-based rollouts to synthesize diverse counterfactual unsafe samples, supporting reliable feasibility identification and feasibility-guided policy learning. Across a range of Safety-Gymnasium tasks with exclusively safe or minimally risky training data, PROCO integrates seamlessly with a variety of offline safe RL algorithms and consistently demonstrates reduced constraint violations and improved safety performance compared to both the original methods and other behavior cloning baselines.

### [227] [Barriers to Counterfactual Credit Attribution for Autoregressive Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01425)
*Aloni Cohen,Chenhao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究生成式AI在信用归因方面的挑战，提出‘反事实信用归因’（CCA）作为确保模型对其输出所依赖的前序工作给予适当信用的技术标准。研究聚焦于自回归模型，发现两种常见方法存在局限：1）对下一个词预测器施加CCA并不能保证整体模型满足CCA，即CCA不具有自回归可组合性；2）提出的‘事后补正’（retrofitting）方法在弱最优条件下存在下界，若仅通过黑盒访问原模型，其查询复杂度随输出长度呈指数增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI在生成内容时往往忽视对先前工作的信用归属，这可能引发学术或法律争议。为解决此问题，需设计一种能自动识别并归因于相关前序数据的生成模型。为此，引入反事实信用归因（CCA）作为形式化目标，旨在确保模型输出不依赖于特定训练数据时仍能正确归因。

Method: 研究采用理论分析方法，探讨自回归生成模型在实现CCA目标时的可行性。通过形式化分析，验证了CCA在自回归结构中的不可组合性，并提出‘ retrofitting’方法进行信用补正，进而建立其在弱最优条件下的查询复杂度下界。

Result: 1）CCA不具备自回归可组合性，即对单个预测步骤施加CCA不能保证整个生成过程满足该属性；2）基于黑盒访问的retrofitting方法在实现CCA时需要指数级查询次数，表明该路径在实际中效率极低。

Conclusion: 当前两种主流实现方式——直接施加于预测器或事后补正——均面临根本性障碍，难以高效构建满足CCA的自回归生成模型。未来需探索新的架构或学习机制以突破这些限制。

Abstract: Generative AI disrupts the practice of giving credit to work that came before. Ideally, a generative model would give credit to any work on which its output depends in a significant way. \emph{Counterfactual credit attribution} (CCA) is a technical condition formalizing this goal--a relaxation of differential privacy--recently introduced by Livni, Moran, Nissim, and Pabbaraju [2024] who studied it in the PAC learning setting.
  We initiate the study of CCA generative models. Specifically, we consider autoregressive models giving credit to a deployment-time dataset (e.g., a RAG database). We uncover barriers to two natural approaches to CCA autoregressive models. First, we show that imposing CCA on the underlying next-token predictor does not guarantee that the model is CCA: CCA does not compose autoregressively (unlike DP). Second, we consider a different approach to building CCA models which we call \emph{retrofitting}. Retrofitting takes a model that does not attribute credit, and adds credit onto it. We prove a lower bound for CCA retrofitting under a weak optimality requirement. Given black-box access to the starting model, retrofitting requires query complexity exponential in the length of the model's outputs.

</details>

*Sunil Kumar Maurya,Xin Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为EstGraph的大图基准数据集，旨在评估大语言模型（LLMs）在有限上下文长度下对大规模图属性的估计能力。针对真实世界中图结构数据规模大且不完全可访问的问题，研究设计了四种任务，并采用基于随机游走采样的提示构造方法，在不超出上下文限制的前提下向模型传递有效信息。实验覆盖多种图数据集，验证了所提方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图推理基准大多局限于小规模图，无法反映真实世界中大规模、部分不可访问图的挑战；随着LLMs推理能力提升，亟需更贴近实际应用场景的评测框架。

Method: 提出EstGraph基准数据集，设计四类估计大图属性的任务；采用随机游走采样技术生成紧凑但信息丰富的提示，以适应LLMs的上下文长度限制。

Result: 所提出的任务与提示策略能有效帮助LLMs在有限上下文中准确估计大规模图的关键属性，展现出较强的泛化能力和实用性。

Conclusion: EstGraph为评估大语言模型在复杂、大规模图数据上的推理能力提供了有效工具，证明了基于采样的提示设计在处理大图问题中的可行性与优越性。

Abstract: With the rapidly improving reasoning abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), there is also a rising demand to use them in a wide variety of domains. This brings about the need to carefully evaluate the limits of the capabilities of these models with various tests and benchmarks. Graph structures are ubiquitous in real-world data, and are often used to represent and analyze relationship patterns within data. Many benchmarks have already been proposed in the graph literature to test the reasoning ability of LLMs to follow and execute graph algorithms. However, due to the limited context length of LLMs, these benchmarks consist of very small graphs. In real-world data, the size of graphs can be significantly larger, and in many cases, not fully accessible. In this paper, we examine a class of problems that arises with very large graphs having limited accessibility. We propose a large graph benchmark dataset, EstGraph, and introduce four distinct tasks designed to estimate large graph properties. We evaluate the reasoning abilities of LLMs on these tasks using a wide variety of graph datasets. In addition, we provide task-specific prompt constructions based on random walk sampling of large graphs (up to millions of nodes) that effectively convey sufficient information to LLMs within the limits of context length.

</details>


### [229] [Protein-Conditioned Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning for Full-Length mRNA Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01513)

TL;DR: ProMORNA 是一个用于从头设计治疗性mRNA的多目标生成框架，通过BART-style模型和多目标相对策略优化（MO-GRPO）在稳定性、翻译效率和免疫安全性之间实现平衡。在萤火虫荧光素酶的案例研究中，其预测的半衰期与翻译效率的联合性能优于传统监督基线，并在功能评分上超越现有先进方法，验证了多目标强化学习在未见靶点mRNA设计中的可行性。

Method: 采用BART风格的编码器-解码器模型在超过600万对天然蛋白-mRNA数据上进行训练，并引入多目标组相对策略优化（MO-GRPO）算法，统一优化多个生物学目标，实现全长度mRNA的生成。

Result: 在萤火虫荧光素酶这一未见靶点上，ProMORNA在计算预测的帕累托前沿上表现出比标准监督基线更优的半衰期与翻译效率组合；同时，在相同评估流程下，其预测功能得分高于当前最先进的基线方法。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了多目标强化学习可用于未见靶点的全长mRNA设计，为治疗性mRNA的高效、安全设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Designing therapeutic messenger RNA (mRNA) requires creating full-length transcripts that carefully balance stability, translation efficiency, and immune safety. To address this challenge, we propose ProMORNA, a multi-objective generation framework that produces complete mRNA transcripts \textit{de novo} directly from a target protein sequence. Our approach begins by training a BART-style encoder-decoder model on over 6 million natural protein-mRNA pairs. We then introduce Multi-Objective Group Relative Policy Optimization (MO-GRPO) to simultaneously optimize for various biological objectives in a unified way. As a case study, we evaluated ProMORNA on the widely used firefly luciferase target, excluding it from both our supervised training data and the prompt pool. The results indicate that ProMORNA improves the \textit{in silico} Pareto frontier for predicted half-life and translation efficiency relative to standard supervised baselines. Additionally, it achieves higher predicted functional scores than a state-of-the-art baseline under the same evaluation pipeline. These computational findings demonstrate the feasibility of using multi-objective reinforcement learning for full-length mRNA design on unseen targets.

### [230] [ECG-biometrics-bench: A Unified Framework for Reproducible Benchmarking of ECG Biometrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01548)
*Milad Parvan*

Main category: cs.LG

Result: 发现随机划分导致性能虚高，真实环境下存在严重性能下降；多种主流模型均表现出类似缺陷，表明问题非模型特定，而是源于当前监督学习范式的固有局限；提出动态多会话模板融合策略可部分缓解时间老化带来的性能退化。

Abstract: Electrocardiogram (ECG) biometrics have emerged as a promising modality for continuous, liveness-aware authentication in wearable systems. However, many prior studies report overly optimistic results due to data leakage (e.g., random splits within the same session). To address this issue, we introduce ECG-biometrics-bench, a modular, reproducible benchmarking framework that standardizes preprocessing, segmentation, and evaluation across seven widely used public ECG datasets spanning clinical, ambulatory, and large-scale cohort settings. The framework supports both closed-set and open-set (i.e., subject-disjoint generalization in this work) evaluation, as well as progressively realistic protocols including cross-session and long-term temporal separation. To facilitate reproducible research in the community, the ECG-biometrics-bench repository will be made publicly accessible on GitHub upon the acceptance of this manuscript. Through a comprehensive multi-dataset analysis, we expose the Random Split Fallacy, demonstrating that intra-session evaluation protocols artificially inflate performance while masking severe degradation caused by temporal drift and unseen identities. Furthermore, by evaluating multiple architectures, including DeepECG, ResNet1D, and CNN-LSTM, we show that these failures are not model-specific but are likely inherent to current supervised feature-learning paradigms. Finally, we demonstrate that performance degradation due to temporal aging can be partially mitigated through a heavy enrollment, lightweight authentication strategy based on dynamic multi-session template fusion. These findings establish a more realistic baseline for ECG biometrics and highlight critical challenges that must be addressed for reliable real-world deployment.

### [231] [Concepts Whisper While Syntax Shouts: Spectral Anti-Concentration and the Dual Geometry of Transformer Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01609)
*Pratyush Acharya,Nuraj Rimal,Habish Dhakal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究检验了Park等人（2024）提出的因果内积是否支持跨语言概念迁移，发现白化因果对齐与仅使用谱正则化无显著差异（p=0.95）。然而，这一失败揭示了一个更广泛的反集中现象：在五种架构家族中，残差流差异均值向量表现出极强的反集中（p<10^{-33}），且得到SAE特征和线性探测的支持。研究发现存在‘双重几何’结构：激活空间的概念方向集中在谱尾，而静态未嵌入行对比则集中在高方差方向（p<10^{-4}）。分裂注入因果干预在Gemma和Llama上验证了功能基础（Cohen's d最高达1.80），8个模型的词性标注探测显示语法偏好编码在高方差子空间（6/8架构，p<0.013），但Qwen 2.5系列出现显著反转，表明架构特异的谱结构。结果暗示变换器可能在上下文处理过程中将语义内容旋转至谱安静区域，以实现低语法干扰的操控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究因果内积在跨语言概念迁移中的有效性，并揭示深层的表征几何结构如何影响概念编码与操纵。

Method: 通过匹配谱随机化测试、反集中分析、SAE特征提取、线性探测、分裂注入因果干预及词性标注探针等方法，系统评估不同模型与语言对中的表征特性。

Result: 白化因果对齐无法超越谱正则化；激活空间概念方向反集中于谱尾，静态未嵌入行对比集中于高方差方向；语法信息优先编码于高方差子空间；部分架构（如Qwen 2.5）出现反常，体现架构依赖的谱结构。

Conclusion: Transformer模型可能通过将语义内容旋转至谱安静区域来实现高效且低干扰的概念操控，表明其内部存在一种双重几何机制，支持语义与语法的解耦编码。

Abstract: We test whether the causal inner product of \citet{park2024linear} -- defined by the unembedding covariance $Σ$ -- enables cross-lingual concept transport. Across 17 models and 4 language pairs, a matched-spectrum randomization test finds that Whitened Causal Alignment is indistinguishable from spectral regularization alone ($p = 0.95$). However, this failure reveals a broader phenomenon: anti-concentration is observed in residual-stream difference-of-means vectors across five architecture families ($p < 10^{-33}$) and supported by SAE features (e.g., $p = 4.5 \times 10^{-19}$) and linear probes on Gemma and Llama. We discover a \emph{dual geometry}: activation-space concept directions anti-concentrate in the spectral tail, while static unembedding-row contrasts \emph{concentrate} in high-variance directions ($p < 10^{-4}$). Split-injection causal interventions support the functional basis on Gemma and Llama (Cohen's $d$ up to $1.80$), and POS-tag probing across 8 models shows syntax preferentially encodes in the high-variance subspace in 6 of 8 architectures ($p < 0.013$), with the Qwen~2.5 family showing a significant reversal consistent with architecture-specific spectral structure. These results suggest transformers may rotate semantic content into spectrally quiet regions during contextualized processing, encoding concepts where they can be manipulated with reduced grammatical disruption.

### [232] [Importance-Guided Basis Selection for Low-Rank Decomposition of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01627)
*Daniel Agyei Asante,Ernie Chang,Yang Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BSI 是一种基于重要性的低秩压缩框架，通过估计移除每个基向量时预期损失的增加来选择保留的奇异向量基。它利用二阶泰勒展开推导出基于导数的重要度评分，结合一阶敏感性和二阶曲率，量化剪枝的影响。为适应大语言模型，提出了一种高效的海森对角线估计器，采用对称参数扰动的Hutchinson随机探测方法。理论分析包括剪枝后的损失增加界、估计误差传播、方差特性与海森谱的关系、高概率样本复杂性保证及扰动强度指导。实验表明，BSI在数学推理基准上持续优于现有最先进方法，尤其在深度压缩下表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低秩压缩方法（如Basel）依赖于下游数据上的奇异值系数重学习并剪枝小幅度基向量，但该启发式策略可能与任务性能不一致，因其忽略了损失景观的局部几何结构。因此需要一种更符合任务目标的基选择机制。

Method: 提出BSI框架，通过二阶泰勒展开计算任务损失关于奇异值的导数，得到基于导数的重要度评分；设计高效海森对角线估计器，利用对称参数扰动的Hutchinson方法实现可扩展性；提供理论支持，涵盖损失增加边界、误差传播、方差分析、样本复杂性与扰动强度建议。

Result: 在数学推理基准上，BSI显著优于现有低秩压缩基线，尤其在深度压缩条件下优势明显，验证了其有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: BSI通过直接建模剪枝对任务损失的影响，实现了更精准的基选择，在保持模型性能的同时大幅降低参数量，是低秩压缩中一种高效且理论完备的新范式。

Abstract: Low-rank decomposition is a compelling approach for compressing large language models, but its effectiveness hinges on selecting which singular-vector bases to retain for a target task. Existing methods such as Basel adapt singular-value coefficients on downstream data and prune bases with small re-learned magnitudes, a heuristic that can be misaligned with task performance because it ignores the local geometry of the loss landscape. We present Basis Selection with Importance (BSI), a principled low-rank compression framework that ranks and prunes bases by directly estimating the expected loss increase incurred when each basis is removed. BSI derives a derivative-based importance score from a second-order Taylor expansion of the task loss with respect to singular values, combining first-order sensitivity and second-order curvature to quantify pruning impact. To make this criterion practical for LLMs, we develop an efficient Hessian-diagonal estimator by adapting the Hutchinson randomized-probing method to loss curvature with symmetric parameter perturbations. We provide a comprehensive theoretical analysis, including loss-increase bounds under basis pruning, explicit propagation of Hessian-diagonal estimation error into these bounds, variance characterization tied to the Hessian spectrum, high-probability sample-complexity guarantees for achieving a target estimation accuracy, and guidance on perturbation intensity. Extensive experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that BSI consistently outperforms state-of-the-art low-rank decomposition baselines, with especially strong improvements under deep compression.

</details>


### [233] [Perturb and Correct: Post-Hoc Ensembles using Affine Redundancy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01632)
*Eleanor Quint*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Perturb-and-Correct (P&C) 是一种后处理方法，通过在隐藏层施加随机扰动并结合最小二乘校正，从单个预训练模型生成具有认知多样性的预测器。该方法在分布内数据上保持一致，在分布外时允许差异，有效平衡了ID/OOD性能，且仅需一个预训练模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型在分布内数据上难以区分，但在分布外表现差异大，亟需一种能生成多样化预测器的方法以提升对分布外数据的鲁棒性与可靠性。

Method: P&C 方法通过在隐藏层引入随机扰动，并在后续仿射层使用最小二乘法进行校正，使预测器在校准数据上保持一致性，而在远离校准分布时产生分歧。其机制通过后校正残差及其一阶敏感性分析实现控制。

Result: P&C 在 MuJoCo 动力学预测和 CIFAR-10 分布外检测任务中均表现出优异的 ID/OOD 平衡能力，性能匹配或超越标准后处理基线，且仅依赖单一预训练模型。

Conclusion: 过参数化可成为深度学习的优势，通过合理利用其多样性潜力，有助于提升模型在分布外场景下的可靠性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Models that are indistinguishable on in-distribution data can behave very differently under distribution shift. We introduce Perturb-and-Correct (P&C), a post-hoc method for constructing epistemically diverse predictors from a single pretrained network. P&C applies random hidden layer perturbations with a least-squares correction in the subsequent affine layer, producing predictors that agree on calibration data while remaining free to disagree away from it. We analyze this mechanism through the post-correction residual and its first-order sensitivity: the residual is controlled near the calibration distribution by a leverage term, while corrected sensitivity grows as inputs deviate from the calibration geometry. Empirically, P&C achieves a strong ID/OOD tradeoff across MuJoCo dynamics prediction and CIFAR-10 OOD detection, matching or outperforming standard post-hoc baselines while requiring only a single pretrained model. Our findings highlight the potential in further exploiting overparameterization as a strength of deep learning models.

</details>


### [234] [Prescriptive Scaling Laws for Data Constrained Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01640)
*Justin Lovelace,Christian Belardi,Srivatsa Kundurthy,Shriya Sudhakar,Kilian Q. Weinberger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 在数据受限的背景下，传统Chinchilla缩放定律因假设每个训练标记都是唯一的，无法有效指导预训练决策。本文提出一种包含附加过拟合惩罚项的新缩放定律，能够准确描述重复数据带来的额外损失，并揭示在一定点后继续重复数据反而有害，计算资源应优先用于提升模型容量。该定律建议的配置在数据受限时可提升性能。此外，由于其单参数形式能将过拟合归一化为一个系数，便于跨配置比较。案例研究表明，强权重衰减（λ=1.0）可使该系数降低约70%，为数据受限下最优权重衰减远高于常规实践的现象提供了缩放定律解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统缩放定律假设所有训练数据唯一，但在数据受限场景下，数据重复普遍存在，导致现有方法难以优化计算资源分配。因此需要新的理论框架来更准确地刻画数据重复对模型性能的影响，并指导实际训练策略。

Method: 引入一个简单的加性过拟合惩罚项，构建新的缩放定律模型，通过实验验证其对重复数据下模型行为的描述能力，并分析不同训练配置下的过拟合系数变化。

Result: 新缩放定律能准确预测数据重复带来的性能下降；在数据受限条件下，按其建议配置可显著提升模型性能；强权重衰减（λ=1.0）可使过拟合系数降低约70%，解释了为何在数据受限时需使用远大于常规的权重衰减值。

Conclusion: 在数据受限的预训练中，过度重复数据会引发过拟合，进一步增加计算投入反而无效。应优先提升模型容量而非重复数据。新提出的缩放定律提供了一种量化过拟合的新方式，支持跨配置比较，并为实际训练中选择更优权重衰减等超参数提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Training compute is increasingly outpacing the availability of high-quality data. This shifts the central challenge from optimal compute allocation to extracting maximum value from limited data. The widely adopted Chinchilla scaling law assumes every training token is unique. This limits its ability to guide pretraining decisions in data-constrained regimes. We model the excess loss under repetition with a simple additive overfitting penalty and find that it accurately describes model behavior. Our scaling law yields qualitatively new compute-optimal allocation advice. Beyond a point, further repetition is counterproductive and compute is better spent on model capacity. We show that following our law's recommended configuration improves performance in data-constrained regimes. Finally, because our one-parameter form isolates overfitting in a single coefficient, it enables direct comparison across training configurations. As a case study, we show that strong weight decay ($λ=1.0$) reduces this coefficient by approximately 70%, providing a scaling-law explanation for recent findings that optimal weight decay in data-constrained regimes is an order of magnitude larger than standard practice.

</details>


### [235] [Geospatial foundation-model embeddings improve population estimation unevenly across space and scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01650)
*Wenbin Zhang,Eimear Cleary,Francisco Rowe,Somnath Chaudhuri,Maksym Bondarenko,Shengjie Lai,Andrew J. Tatem*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究评估了地理空间基础模型（PDFM）在巴西、尼日利亚和美国的次国家级人口估计中的表现，发现其相比传统地理空间协变量可显著提升预测精度，尤其在数据匮乏、发展水平较低的地区。然而，其性能受空间尺度不匹配的限制，跨尺度迁移能力较弱，揭示了当前地理空间人工智能的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有次国家级人口估计依赖于手工构建的地理空间协变量（如聚落范围、夜间灯光等），这些数据在普查稀疏、过时或空间分辨率粗糙的地区难以获取且需跨区域协调。为解决这一问题，本文探索使用地理空间基础模型学习更通用的场所表征，以提升人口估计的可靠性。

Method: 通过对比地理空间基础模型（PDFM）嵌入与传统地理空间协变量，在巴西、尼日利亚和美国三个国家进行次国家级人口估计的基准测试；采用结构化地理验证方法评估模型在不同国家-模型组合下的预测性能，并分析其在不同空间尺度下的表现差异。

Result: PDFM在多数情况下显著提升了预测拟合度，中位数降低未解释方差20.1%（四分位距：10.0%-33.2%），并减少23.2%的Kullback-Leibler散度（9.2%-26.2%）。但在空间尺度不一致时性能下降明显，表明其跨尺度迁移能力有限。

Conclusion: 地理空间基础模型能有效提升数据贫乏地区的次国家级人口估计精度，但其性能受限于空间尺度匹配程度，反映出当前地理空间人工智能在泛化能力上的根本缺陷。

Abstract: Reliable subnational population estimates are essential for applications, yet remain difficult where censuses are sparse, outdated or spatially coarse. Existing population-mapping workflows rely on hand-built geospatial covariates, such as settlement extent, night-time lights, and environmental conditions, which must be assembled and harmonised across scales and geographies. Geospatial foundation models offer an alternative by learning reusable representations of place from more multifaceted and heterogeneous data sources. Here, we benchmark Population Dynamics Foundation Model (PDFM) embeddings against the harmonised geospatial covariates for subnational population estimation in Brazil, Nigeria and the United States. Under geographically structured validation, PDFM increased predictive fit by a median of 20.1% (IQR: 10.0-33.2%, across country-model comparisons) reduction in unexplained variance, and reduced Kullback-Leibler divergence by 23.2% (9.2-26.2%). However, these gains were uneven. PDFM was most advantageous where the geospatial covariates weakly characterised settlement context, such as larger and less-developed subnational areas. Moreover, PDFM performance was scale-coupled with embeddings providing less flexible transfer across spatial aggregations than geospatial covariates. These findings showed that geospatial foundation-model representations of place can improve population estimation in data poor settings, but their benefits break down predictably under spatial scale mismatch, revealing a fundamental limitation of current geospatial AI.

</details>


### [236] [Towards Efficient and Expressive Offline RL via Flow-Anchored Noise-conditioned Q-Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01663)
*Sungyoung Lee,Dohyeong Kim,Eshan Balachandar,Zelal Su Mustafaoglu,Keshav Pingali*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FAN是一种高效且高性能的离线强化学习算法，通过仅使用一次流策略迭代和单个高斯噪声样本，显著降低了计算成本，同时保持甚至提升了性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在使用表达性强的流策略和分布式评论家时虽然性能优越，但计算成本过高，特别是流策略需要多次采样生成动作，分布式评论家也需要对多个样本（如分位数）进行计算。为解决这些效率问题，提出更高效的替代方案。

Method: 提出Flow-Anchored Noise-conditioned Q-Learning (FAN)，采用行为正则化技术，仅需一次流策略迭代和一个高斯噪声样本即可完成分布式评论家的估计，从而大幅降低计算开销。

Result: 在机器人操作和运动控制任务上的实验表明，FAN实现了最先进的性能，并显著减少了训练和推理时间。代码已开源。

Conclusion: FAN通过简化计算流程，在不牺牲性能的前提下显著提升了离线强化学习的效率，是高效与高性能兼具的先进算法。

Abstract: We propose Flow-Anchored Noise-conditioned Q-Learning (FAN), a highly efficient and high-performing offline reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm. Recent work has shown that expressive flow policies and distributional critics improve offline RL performance, but at a high computational cost. Specifically, flow policies require iterative sampling to produce a single action, and distributional critics require computation over multiple samples (e.g., quantiles) to estimate value. To address these inefficiencies while maintaining high performance, we introduce FAN. Our method employs a behavior regularization technique that utilizes only a single flow policy iteration and requires only a single Gaussian noise sample for distributional critics. Our theoretical analysis of convergence and performance bounds demonstrates that these simplifications not only improve efficiency but also lead to superior task performance. Experiments on robotic manipulation and locomotion tasks demonstrate that FAN achieves state-of-the-art performance while significantly reducing both training and inference runtimes. We release our code at https://github.com/brianlsy98/FAN.

</details>
